# 5 Decomposition of Generative AI Exposure: Methods

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 5 生成式 AI 暴露的分解：方法

接下来，我们将分解总 generative AI【待定】暴露（Generative AI Exposure【待定】）的变动，以识别劳动力需求（labor demand【待定】）随时间变化的边际。我们的核心区分在于两种调整形式。企业可以通过在不同类型工作岗位之间重新分配招聘信息（postings）来改变其招聘地点。它们还可以通过修改可比工作的任务内容来改变工作岗位的内容。第一个边际是招聘重新分配（hiring reallocation【待定】）；第二个是岗位重新设计（job redesign【待定】）。我们的主要分析使用了 Kitagawa 分解（Kitagawa, 1955）的三重扩展（three-fold【待定】）。该分解将总暴露的变动分解为三个组成部分的加总：构成效应、单元内（within-cell【待定】）暴露效应和交互效应。构成效应捕捉所发布工作组合的变动。单元内暴露效应捕捉可比工作内部暴露的变动。交互效应捕捉当这两种调整同时发生时产生的额外变动。我们以基于回归的 Oaxaca–Blinder 分解（Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition【待定】）（Oaxaca, 1973; Blinder, 1973; Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025）来补充 Kitagawa 分析。这两种分解相互关联但目的不同。Kitagawa 分解提供了基于单元（cell）的总体暴露变动的核算。而 Oaxaca–Blinder 分解则询问哪些可观察的工作特征（如职业、行业、资历、地点、远程工作状态（remote-work status【待定】）、实习状态和雇佣类型）与 GPT 前（pre-GPT【待定】）和 GPT 后（post-GPT【待定】）时期之间的暴露缺口最为相关。因此，Kitagawa 识别调整边际，而 Oaxaca–Blinder 有助于描述构成变化发生的可观察维度。

【本段术语】
- Generative AI Exposure: Generative AI Exposure【待定】
- labor demand: labor demand【待定】
- hiring reallocation: hiring reallocation【待定】
- job redesign: job redesign【待定】
- three-fold: three-fold【待定】
- within-cell: within-cell【待定】
- Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition: Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition【待定】
- pre-GPT: pre-GPT【待定】
- post-GPT: post-GPT【待定】
- remote-work status: remote-work status【待定】
- Kitagawa decomposition: 菊川分解（未在术语表中，正常翻译）
- composition effect: 构成效应（未在术语表中）
- within-cell exposure effect: within-cell exposure effect【待定】（整体视为术语，但术语表仅有 within-cell，此处照录并标注）
- interaction effect: 交互效应（未在术语表）
- Oaxaca–Blinder: Oaxaca–Blinder（已含 decomposition 术语）

【本段要点】
- 核心区分两种调整边际：招聘重新分配（跨岗位类型）和岗位重新设计（修改任务内容）。
- 主要方法：Kitagawa 三重分解，将总暴露变化分解为构成效应、单元内暴露效应和交互效应。
- 补充方法：Oaxaca–Blinder 分解，识别哪些可观察工作特征（如职业、行业、地点等）与暴露缺口相关。
- 两者关系：Kitagawa 提供以单元为基础的核算，Oaxaca–Blinder 描述构成变化发生的具体维度。

【可能需人工复核】
- “within-cell exposure effect” 整体作为术语处理，术语表中仅有 “within-cell”，是否应拆分？此处保留整体并标注【待定】。
- “labor demand” 在原文中为连续单词 “labordemandchanges”，已按上下文拆分翻译，请确认准确性。
- “internship status” 和 “employment type” 未出现在术语表，直接翻译为 “实习状态” 和 “雇佣类型”，无需标注。
- “Kitagawa decomposition” 及 “Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition” 中的引文信息保持原样，未翻译为中文姓名。

## English

# 5 Decomposition of Generative AI Exposure: Methods

We next decompose changes in aggregate generative AI exposure to identify the margins through whichlabordemandchangesovertime. Ourcentraldistinctionisbetweentwoformsofadjustment. Firmsmaychangewheretheyhirebyreallocatingpostingsacrossdifferenttypesofjobs. Theymay also change what jobs contain by revising the task content of comparable jobs. The first margin is hiring reallocation; the second is job redesign. Our main analysis uses a three-fold extension of the Kitagawa decomposition (Kitagawa, 1955). This decomposition expresses changes in aggregate exposure as the sum of three components: a composition effect, a within-cell exposure effect, and an interaction effect. The composition effect captures changes in the mix of posted jobs. The within-cell exposure effect captures changes in exposure within comparable jobs. The interaction effect captures the additional change that arises when these two adjustments occur simultaneously. We complement the Kitagawa analysis with a regression-based Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition (Oaxaca, 1973; Blinder, 1973; Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025). The two decompositions are related but serve different purposes. The Kitagawa decomposition provides a cell-based accounting of aggregate exposure changes. The Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition instead asks which observable job characteristics, such as occupation, industry, seniority, location, remote-work status, internship status, and employment type, are most associated with the exposure gap between the pre- and post-GPT periods. Thus, Kitagawa identifies the adjustment margins, while Oaxaca–Blinder helps characterize the observable dimensions along which compositional change occurs.

# 5.1 Cell-Level Representation of Aggregate Exposure

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 5.1 工作单元层面的总体接触度表征

我们的接触度衡量指标定义在招聘帖层面。为研究总体劳动力需求调整，我们将招聘帖层面的接触度汇总至工作单元。一个工作单元由职业、资历和行业共同定义。这种单元结构与我们抽样策略的主要维度相匹配，并捕捉了研究设计中三个关键的异质性来源：所执行工作的类型、工作所处的部门以及职位的职业阶段。令 βₚ 表示招聘帖 p 的帖子层面接触度指标，t 表示时间段。总体接触度在时期 t 为所有该时期招聘帖接触度的平均值：Ēₜ = E[βₚ | t]。由于每个招聘帖属于唯一且互斥的工作单元 c，总体接触度可写作单元层面接触度的加权平均值：
Ēₜ = Σₛ E[βₚ | c, t] Pr(c | t)。    (5)
定义 E_{c,t} = E[βₚ | c, t] 为时期 t 内工作单元 c 的平均接触度，w_{c,t} = Pr(c | t) 为时期 t 内属于工作单元 c 的招聘帖比例。则总体接触度可写作：
Ēₜ = Σₛ w_{c,t} E_{c,t}。    (6)

方程(6)表明，总体接触度可通过两个基本边际发生变化。第一，企业可能改变其发布的职位组合，这会改变权重 w_{c,t}。第二，可比职位的任务内容可能随时间变化，这会改变 E_{c,t}。在我们的解释中，第一个边际捕捉了不同工作单元之间的招聘重新配置，第二个边际则捕捉了单元内部的职位再设计。令时期 0 为基准期。在我们的主要实施中，时期 0 为整个 2021 年。我们以 2021 年作为基准，因为该年处于生成式 AI 工具广泛公开传播之前，并提供了一个稳定的 GPT 前基准。我们的目标是将时期 0 与时期 t 之间总体接触度的变化进行分解：
ΔĞₜ = Ēₜ − Ē₀。    (7)

【本段要点】
- 将招聘帖层面的接触度汇总到由职业、资历、行业定义的工作单元，形成单元结构。
- 总体接触度可以表示为单元层面接触度的加权平均，权重为各时期各单元的招聘帖比例。
- 总体接触度的变化通过两个边际实现：企业调整职位组合（招聘重新配置）和职位任务内容变化（工作再设计）。
- 选取2021年作为基准期，因其在生成式AI广泛传播之前，可作为稳定的GPT前基准。
- 核心目标是分解基准期与目标期之间总体接触度的变化。

## English

# 5.1 Cell-Level Representation of Aggregate Exposure

Ourexposuremeasureisdefinedatthepostinglevel. Tostudyaggregatelabor-demandadjustment, we aggregate posting-level exposure to job cells. A cell is defined by occupation, seniority, and industry. This cell structure matches the main dimensions of our sampling strategy and captures three sources of heterogeneity central to our research design: the type of work being performed, the sector in which it is performed, and the career stage of the job. Let β denote the posting-level exposure measure for posting p, and let t index time periods. p Aggregate exposure in period t is the average exposure across postings in that period: E¯ = E[β | t]. t p Because every posting belongs to one mutually exclusive cell c, aggregate exposure can be written as a weighted average of cell-level exposure: X E¯ = E[β | c, t]Pr(c | t). (5) t p c Define E ≡ E[β | c, t] as mean exposure within cell c in period t, and w ≡ Pr(c | t) as the c, t p c, t share of postings in period t that belong to cell c. Then aggregate exposure can be written as X E¯ = w E. (6) t c, t c, t c Equation (6) shows that aggregate exposure can change through two basic margins. First, firms may change the mix of jobs they post, which changes the weights w. Second, the task content of c, t comparable jobs may change over time, which changes E. In our interpretation, the first margin c, t captures hiring reallocation across job cells, while the second captures job redesign within cells. Let period 0 denote the baseline period. In our main implementation, period 0 is the full year 2021. We use year 2021 as the baseline because it precedes the broad public diffusion of generative AI tools and provides a stable pre-GPT benchmark. Our goal is to decompose the change in aggregate exposure between period 0 and period t: ∆E¯ = E¯ −E¯. (7) t t 0

# 5.2 Three-Fold Kitagawa Decomposition

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 5.2 三重木场分解法

我们将总暴露度的变化分解为三个反事实成分：

X X X ∆E¯ = (w −w)E + w (E −E) + (w −w)(E −E). (8) t c, t c, 0 c, 0 c, 0 c, t c, 0 c, t c, 0 c, t c, 0 |c {z } |c {z } |c {z } 构成效应 单元内暴露度效应 交互效应

第一项是构成效应。它衡量如果招聘岗位份额从2021年的分布转变为时期t的分布，而每个单元内的暴露度保持在2021年水平不变，总暴露度将如何变化。实质上，这一项捕捉了跨职位单元的招聘再配置。正值表示招聘岗位正转向在基准期对生成式AI暴露度更高的单元。负值表示招聘岗位正远离这些暴露度较高的单元。

第二项是单元内暴露度效应。它衡量如果单元级暴露度从2021年水平转变为时期t水平，而招聘岗位份额保持在2021年分布不变，总暴露度将如何变化。实质上，这一项捕捉了同类职位内的职位重新设计。负值表示在保持基准招聘岗位分布不变的情况下，单元内描述的任务随时间推移对生成式AI的暴露度有所降低。正值表示单元内任务内容向更高暴露度方向移动。

第三项是交互效应。它捕捉因招聘岗位份额和单元内暴露度同时变动而产生的额外变化。这一项表明招聘再配置与职位重新设计是相互强化还是相互抵消。例如，当招聘岗位转向暴露度下降的单元，或远离暴露度上升的单元时，交互项为负。当两种变动共同推动总暴露度朝同一方向时，交互项为正。

这种三重分解公式在我们这里很有用，因为它分别识别了企业招聘地点的变化、同类职位内容的变化以及这两者的联合变动。经典的双重木场分解将交互项分配到构成效应和单元内成分中。我们在附录G中报告相应的双重分解结果。

- Three-Fold Kitagawa Decomposition: 三重木场分解法

- within-cell exposure effect: 单元内暴露度效应
- interaction effect: 交互效应
- aggregate exposure: 总暴露度
- posting shares: 招聘岗位份额
- hiring reallocation: 招聘再配置
- job redesign: 职位重新设计
- two-fold: 双重
- Kitagawa decomposition: 木场分解
- generative AI: 生成式AI
- baseline period: 基准期
- within-cell: 单元内
- occupation-level: 职位级别（本段未直接出现但相关）
- task-level: 任务级别

【本段要点】
- 将总暴露度变化分解为三个反事实成分：构成效应、单元内暴露度效应和交互效应。
- 构成效应衡量岗位份额变化带来的影响，反映招聘再配置；正值表示转向高暴露度单元，负值反之。
- 单元内暴露度效应衡量单元级暴露度变化的影响，反映职位重新设计；负值表示任务暴露度降低，正值反之。
- 交互效应捕捉份额与暴露度同时变动的额外影响，表明招聘再配置与职位重新设计是相互强化还是抵消。
- 三重分解分别识别招聘地点变化、职位内容变化及其联合变动，优于将交互项分配至前两者的双重分解。

- 公式中的符号和下标（如 w_c, t 等）需要保持与原文一致，中文译文已保留原公式形式，但需确认数学表达式在Markdown中是否正确呈现。
- “Kitagawa decomposition”译为“木场分解”是否准确？通常为“木场分解”或“北川分解”，此处采用前者，需确认学界常用译法。
- “within-cell exposure”译为“单元内暴露度”，术语表中“within-cell”待定，此处暂译，需对照原文用法统一。
- “period-t”和“2021 level”等时间表述的准确性，注意原文中的下标0和t分别对应2021年和时期t。
- “job redesign”译为“职位重新设计”，与“job redesign within comparable jobs”对应，需确保上下文一致性。

## English

# 5.2 Three-Fold Kitagawa Decomposition

We decompose the change in aggregate exposure into three counterfactual components:

X X X ∆E¯ = (w −w)E + w (E −E) + (w −w)(E −E). (8) t c, t c, 0 c, 0 c, 0 c, t c, 0 c, t c, 0 c, t c, 0 |c {z } |c {z } |c {z } Compositioneffect Within-cellexposureeffect Interactioneffect The first term is the composition effect. It measures how aggregate exposure would change if posting shares shifted from their 2021 distribution to their period-t distribution, while exposure withineachcellremainedfixedatits2021level. Substantively, thistermcaptureshiringreallocation across job cells. A positive value means that postings are shifting toward cells that were more exposed to generative AI in the baseline period. A negative value means that postings are shifting away from those more exposed cells. The second term is the within-cell exposure effect. It measures how aggregate exposure would change if cell-level exposure shifted from its 2021 level to its period-t level, while posting shares remained fixed at their 2021 distribution. Substantively, this term captures job redesign within comparable jobs. A negative value indicates that the tasks described within a cell have become less exposed to generative AI over time, holding the baseline distribution of postings fixed. A positive value indicates movement toward more exposed task content within cells. The third term is the interaction effect. It captures the additional change that arises because posting shares and within-cell exposure move at the same time. This term indicates whether hiring reallocation and job redesign reinforce or offset each other. For example, the interaction term is negative when postings shift toward cells whose exposure is falling, or away from cells whose exposure is rising. It is positive when the two movements push aggregate exposure in the same direction. This three-fold formulation is useful in our setting because it separately identifies changes in where firms hire, changes in what comparable jobs contain, and the joint movement of the two. The classic two-fold Kitagawa decomposition allocates the interaction term into the composition and within-cell components. We report the corresponding two-fold decomposition in Appendix G.

# 5.3 Common Support and Robustness of the Decomposition

## 中文

【中文译文】

# 5.3 共同支撑与分解的稳健性

观测到的单元格集合会随时间变化。某些职业-资历-行业单元格可能在基期出现，但在后续时期消失，反之亦然。为确保分解比较的是可比的单元格，我们将基年与时期 t 之间的时期特定共同支撑定义为 S = {c: w_{c,0} > 0 且 w_{c,t} > 0}。单元格 c 在 2021 年和时期 t 中均被观测到。在应用分解之前，我们在该共同支撑样本中重新标准化职位发布份额。这种方法将分析聚焦于持续性职位单元格的变化，而非机械地将变化归因于单元格的进入或退出。由于重新标准化后的共同支撑总量与原始总量并不相同，

- common-support: [待定]
- occupation-by-seniority-by-industry cells: [待定]

- re-normalize: [待定]

【本段要点】
- 单元格集合可能随时间变化，导致某些单元格仅在特定时期存在。
- 定义共同支撑集 S，仅包含基年和目标时期 t 均出现的单元格。
- 在共同支撑样本中对职位发布份额重新标准化，再执行分解。
- 此方法聚焦于持续性岗位的变化，避免将变化机械归因于单元格的进出。
- 重新标准化后的总量与原总量不同，需注意该差异。

- 术语“occupation-by-seniority-by-industry cells”中的“cells”在上下文中指“单元格”，但中文表达可考虑“单元”或“格子”，此处按学术惯例译为“单元格”。

- 最后一句未完成，但译文按原文结构处理，保留“并不相同”的省略感。

## English

# 5.3 Common Support and Robustness of the Decomposition

The set of observed cells can vary over time. Some occupation-by-seniority-by-industry cells may appearinthebaselineperiodbutnotinalaterperiod, orviceversa. Toensurethatthedecompositioncomparescomparablecells, wedefinetheperiod-specificcommonsupportbetweenthebaseline

year and period t as S = {c: w > 0 and w > 0}. t c, 0 c, t Cells in S are observed in both 2021 and period t. We re-normalize posting shares within this t common-support sample before applying the decomposition. This approach focuses the analysis on changes among persistent job cells, rather than mechanically attributing changes to cell entry or exit. Because the re-normalized common-support aggregate is not identical to the raw aggregate,

## 中文

【中文译文】
附录F报告了重叠诊断、重建检验以及原始序列与重新归一化后的总序列之间的差异。这些诊断表明，共同支撑序列紧密追踪原始总序列，且重建差异可忽略不计。正文中报告了方程（8）的三重分解。附录G报告了另外两项分析。首先，我们实施了对称的两重北川（Kitagawa）分解，该方法通过将交互项均匀分配至组成成分和单元内成分两部分，将总变化分解为组成变化和单元内变化。其次，我们使用一个平衡单元样本（仅包含在整个样本期内均存在的单元）重复了分析。这些分析证实，主要模式并非由交互项的处理方式或单元支撑随时间的变化所驱动。

【可能需人工复核】
- “common-support series”译为“共同支撑序列”，需确认术语是否准确。
- “raw aggregate”译为“原始总序列”，需与领域惯例核对。
- “two-fold Kitagawa decomposition”明确为两重北川分解，但“Kitagawa”的中译是常见音译，需检查是否采用标准译名（如“北川”）。
- “cell support”译为“单元支撑”，需确认是否贴合上下文含义（指单元在时间上的存在性）。

## English

# Appendix F reports overlap diagnostics, reconstruction checks, and the gap between the raw and

re-normalized aggregate series. These diagnostics show that the common-support series closely tracks the raw aggregate and that the reconstruction gap is negligible. Our main text reports the three-fold decomposition in Equation (8). Appendix G reports two additional exercises. First, we implement the symmetric two-fold Kitagawa decomposition, which separates aggregate change into composition and within-cell components by allocating the interaction term evenly across the two. Second, we repeat the analysis using a balanced-cell sample restricted to cells observed throughout the full sample period. These analyses confirm that the main patterns are not driven by the treatment of the interaction term or by changes in cell support over time.

# 5.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition

## 中文

【中文译文】

# 5.4 奥克萨卡-布林德分解（Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition）

北川分解（Kitagawa decomposition）将总体的暴露变化分解为重新分配、重新设计和交互作用三个部分。然而，它并未识别出哪些可观测的工作特征与暴露差距关联最大。例如，一个较大的构成效应可能反映了职业、行业、资历组、地点、远程工作安排或就业类型之间的转变。为了检验这些可观测维度，我们用基于回归的奥克萨卡-布林德分解（Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition）来补充北川分析（Oaxaca, 1973; Blinder, 1973; Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025）。奥克萨卡-布林德分解比较了两个总时期：GPT之前时期（pre-GPT period）和GPT之后时期（post-GPT period）。它将平均暴露的变化分解为可解释部分（explained component）和不可解释部分（unexplained component）。可解释部分捕捉了与可观测工作特征变化相关的部分。不可解释部分则捕捉了与这些特征和暴露之间关系的变化以及未观测因素相关的剩余部分。

为了计算上的可操作性，我们在单元层级（cell level）实施该分解。每个单元由职业、资历和行业的唯一组合定义。回归按每个单元-时期的招聘信息数量进行加权，从而使估计结果再现招聘信息层级的矩。估计方程为：
′ Y = α + X β + ε, (9)
c, g g c, g g c, g
其中 g ∈ {A, B} 表示GPT之前和GPT之后时期，Y 是单元 c 和时期组 g 的平均暴露，X 是可观测工作特征向量。协变量按模块组织：职业、行业、资历、州、远程工作安排、实习状态和就业类型。职业模块包含样本中观察到的923个O*NET–SOC类别；行业模块包含20个两位数NAICS部门；资历模块包括初级、中级和高级招聘信息；州模块包括51个州类别；远程工作模块包括远程、混合和非远程招聘信息；实习模块区分实习生和非实习生招聘信息；就业类型模块包括全职、兼职和兼职/全职招聘信息。每个模块省略一个参考类别后，该规范包含约1000个回归变量。使用GPT之前时期作为参考结构，两重分解（two-fold decomposition）为：
Yˉ −Yˉ = (Xˉ −Xˉ)′ β̂ + (α̂ −α̂) + Xˉ′ (β̂ −β̂). (10)
B A | B A A | B A B B A
可解释部分 不可解释部分

可解释部分回答了一个反事实问题：如果可观测工作特征的分布从GPT之前时期转变为GPT之后时期，而这些特征与暴露之间的关联仍固定在其GPT之前时期的水平上，那么平均暴露会改变多少？因此，它捕捉了暴露差距中可归因于可观测工作特征变化的部分。这一部分在概念上与北川构成效应相关，因为两者都涉及构成变化。然而，在我们的实现中，这两个对象并不完全相同。北川构成效应是一个基于单元的核算项，计算时覆盖了完整的职业×行业×资历单元集。而奥克萨卡-布林德可解释部分是一个

## English

# 5.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition

The Kitagawa decomposition separates aggregate exposure changes into reallocation, redesign, and interaction components. It does not, however, identify which observable job characteristics are most associated with the exposure gap. For example, a large composition effect may reflect shifts across occupations, industries, seniority groups, locations, remote-work arrangements, or employmenttypes. Toexaminetheseobservabledimensions, wecomplementtheKitagawaanalysis with a regression-based Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition (Oaxaca, 1973; Blinder, 1973; Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025). The Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition compares two aggregate periods: the pre-GPT period and the post-GPT period. It decomposes the change in mean exposure into an explained component and an unexplained component. The explained component captures the portion associated with changes in observable job characteristics. The unexplained component captures the remaining

portion associated with changes in the relationship between those characteristics and exposure, as well as unobserved factors. We implement the decomposition at the cell level for computational tractability. Each cell is defined by a unique combination of occupation, seniority, and industry. The regression is weighted bythenumberofpostingsineachcell-periodsothattheestimatesreproduceposting-levelmoments. The estimating equation is ′ Y = α +X β +ε, (9) c, g g c, g g c, g where g ∈ {A, B} indexes the pre- and post-GPT periods, Y is mean exposure in cell c and c, g period group g, and X is a vector of observable job characteristics. The covariates are organized c, g into blocks: occupation, industry, seniority, state, remote-work arrangement, internship status, and employment type. The occupation block includes 923 O*NET–SOC categories observed in our sample; the industry block includes 20 two-digit NAICS sectors; the seniority block includes junior, intermediate, and senior postings; the state block includes 51 state categories; the remote-work block includes remote, hybrid, and not-remote postings; the internship block distinguishes intern from non-intern postings; and the employment-type block includes full-time, part-time, and parttime/full-time postings. After omitting one reference category per block, the specification includes approximately 1, 000 regressors. Using the pre-GPT period as the reference structure, the two-fold decomposition is Y¯ −Y¯ = (X¯ −X¯)′ βˆ +(αˆ −αˆ)+X¯′ (βˆ −βˆ). (10) B A | B {z A A} | B A {z B B A} Explained Unexplained Theexplainedcomponentanswersacounterfactualquestion: howmuchwouldaverageexposure change if the distribution of observable job characteristics shifted from the pre-GPT period to the post-GPT period, while the association between those characteristics and exposure remained fixed at its pre-GPT level? It therefore captures the part of the exposure gap attributable to shifts in observed job characteristics. This component is conceptually related to the Kitagawa composition effect because both involve changes in composition. However, the two objects are not identical in our implementation. The Kitagawa composition effect is a cell-based accounting term computed over the full set of occupation-by-industry-by-seniority cells. The Oaxaca–Blinder explained component is a

# 5.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 5.4 奥克斯卡-布林德分解

基于回归的分解方法，将可观测特征作为可加协变量块纳入模型。如果奥克斯卡-布林德模型设定完全饱和，即包含与北川分解所用完全相同的单元格指标，那么其解释部分将紧密对应于北川分解的构成效应（Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025）。本研究则将奥克斯卡-布林德分解作为一种补充性诊断工具：它识别出哪些可观测特征能够解释与构成差异相关的暴露度变化。其中，未解释部分则反映了在考虑可观测职位特征变化后剩余的暴露度差距。形式上，该部分体现了GPT前与GPT后时期截距项和估计系数的变化。本研究不将其解释为北川分解中单元格内效应的直接类比。该部分的大小取决于参照组的选择、纳入的协变量以及回归的函数形式（Fortin et al., 2011）。因此，本研究将其解释为可观测职位特征变化未能解释的暴露度差距部分，而非职位重新设计的独立度量。本研究仅报告解释部分的详细贡献，且仅限于协变量块层面。这一选择遵循分解分析的标准做法。对于分类变量，某一协变量块（如职业或行业）的总贡献不受遗漏参照类别选择的影响。相比之下，块内单个类别的贡献则取决于哪个类别被省略；改变参照类别可能会在类别间重新分配贡献，但不改变块总贡献（Fortin et al., 2011）。因此，本研究报告的是块层面的解释贡献，例如职业、行业或资历的总贡献。对于未解释部分，类别层面的贡献对参照组的选择更为敏感，因为它们衡量的是相对于省略类别的系数变化。因此，本研究仅从整体层面解读未解释部分。

【本段术语】
- Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition: 奥克斯卡-布林德分解
- Kitagawa decomposition: 北川分解
- explained component: 解释部分
- unexplained component: 未解释部分
- within-cell effect: 单元格内效应
- composition effect: 构成效应
- exposure gap: 暴露度差距
- job redesign: 职位重新设计
- covariate blocks: 协变量块
- pre-GPT: GPT前时期
- post-GPT: GPT后时期
- block-level: 块层面
- category-level: 类别层面
- reference category: 参照类别

【本段要点】
- 奥克斯卡-布林德分解作为补充诊断工具，用于识别解释暴露度变化的可观测特征。
- 未解释部分反映可观测特征变化无法解释的暴露度差距，但不等同于北川分解的单元格内效应。
- 解释部分仅报告协变量块层面的贡献，以避免遗漏参照类别的选择问题。
- 未解释部分仅从整体层面解读，因类别层面贡献对参照组选择高度敏感。

【可能需人工复核】
- 本段中“GPT前时期”与“GPT后时期”的翻译是否准确？原文为“pre-GPT”和“post-GPT”，术语表中标记为[待定]，但根据上下文应为GPT发布前后的时期。
- “北川分解”是否对应“Kitagawa decomposition”？术语表中未列出，但为常见译法，需确认。
- “暴露度差距”是否恰当地表达了“exposure gap”？原文背景为AI暴露度，需结合领域知识确认。

## English

# 5.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition

regression-based decomposition that enters observable characteristics as additive covariate blocks. If the Oaxaca–Blinder specification were fully saturated with indicators for the exact same cells used in the Kitagawa decomposition, the explained component would closely correspond to the Kitagawa composition effect (Oaxaca and Sierminska, 2025). Our implementation instead uses the Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition as a complementary diagnostic tool: it identifies which observable characteristics account for the exposure change associated with compositional differences. The unexplained component captures the remaining exposure gap after accounting for changes in observed job characteristics. Formally, it reflects changes in the intercept and in the estimated coeﬀicients between the pre- and post-GPT periods. We do not interpret this component as a direct analog of the Kitagawa within-cell effect. Its magnitude depends on the choice of reference group, the included covariates, and the functional form of the regression (Fortin et al., 2011). We therefore interpret it as the portion of the exposure gap not accounted for by shifts in observable job characteristics, rather than as a separate measure of job redesign. We report detailed contributions only for the explained component and only at the level of covariate blocks. This choice follows standard practice in decomposition analysis. For categorical variables, the total contribution of a block, such as occupation or industry, is invariant to the choice of omitted reference category. In contrast, contributions of individual categories within a block depend on which category is omitted; changing the reference category can redistribute contributions across categories without changing the block total (Fortin et al., 2011). We therefore report block-level explained contributions, such as the total contribution of occupation, industry, or seniority. For the unexplained component, category-level contributions are even more sensitive to the choice of reference group because they measure coeﬀicient changes relative to the omitted category. We therefore interpret the unexplained component only in the aggregate.

# 6 Results

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 6 结果

本节呈现了分解结果。我们首先报告三重基塔加瓦分解，该分解将总体生成式AI暴露度的变化分解为招聘再分配、单元内工作重新设计以及两者的交互作用。接着，我们检验这些边际效应是否随职业阶梯层级而有所不同。最后，我们报告一种补充性的瓦哈卡-布林德分解，以识别哪些可观测的工作特征与GPT前后暴露度差距最为相关。

This section presents the decomposition results. We first report the three-fold Kitagawa decomposition, whichseparateschangesinaggregategenerativeAIexposureintohiringreallocation, withincell job redesign, and their interaction. observable job characteristics are most associated with the pre- versus post-GPT exposure gap.

## English

# Figure 6 presents the three-fold Kitagawa decomposition of changes in mean exposure relative to

the 2021 baseline. The black line shows the total change in aggregate exposure. The bars separate this change into three components: a composition effect, a within-cell exposure effect, and an interaction effect. In substantive terms, the composition effect captures changes in where firms hire, the within-cell exposure effect captures changes in what comparable jobs contain, and the interaction effect captures the joint movement of these two margins.

# Figure 6: Three-Fold Decomposition of Changes in Aggregate Generative AI Exposure

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 图6：生成式AI总体暴露变化的三重分解

注释：该图展示了与2021年基线相比，总体暴露变化的三重喜多川（Kitagawa）分解。黑色线条表示总体暴露的总变化。条形图显示了构成效应、单元内暴露效应及其交互作用的贡献。总体暴露相对于2021年基线在2023年初上升，随后在2023年第三季度开始转为负值，并在样本期末持续下降。分解结果表明，这一转折点反映了两个边际的变化。在2023年第三季度之前，构成效应普遍为正，表明招聘帖子的组合向基线暴露程度更高的职位单元转移。从该季度开始，构成效应转为负值，表明招聘需求从2021年暴露程度较高的单元转移开。这一模式与招聘需求从暴露程度较高的工作岗位重新分配的现象一致。单元内暴露效应则呈现出不同的轨迹。它在2023年第三季度之前接近于零，随后变得越来越负。由于这一成分是在“行业×职业×资历”单元内测量的，它捕捉的是可比职位之间的暴露变化，而非广泛职业类别的组合变化。因此，其下降表明雇主修改了其继续发布的职位的工作任务内容，从而降低了这些职位对生成式AI的暴露程度。这就是静态职业层面暴露测量无法观察到的“工作重新设计”边际。

【本段要点】
- 图6使用三重喜多川分解展示总体生成式AI暴露相对于2021年基线的变化。
- 总体暴露在2023年初上升，2023年第三季度后转为持续下降，构成效应和单元内暴露效应均驱动了这一转折。
- 构成效应在2023年第三季度前为正（招聘转向高暴露单元），之后为负（招聘从高暴露单元转移），与招聘需求再分配一致。
- 单元内暴露效应在2023年第三季度前接近零，之后持续为负，表明雇主在同类职位中通过调整任务内容降低暴露——这是静态职业层面测量无法捕捉的“工作重新设计”边际。

【可能需人工复核】
- “三重喜多川分解”在中文文献中通常译为“三重分解”或“喜多川分解”，但术语表要求待定，此处暂译，需根据领域惯例确认。
- “occupation-by-industry-by-seniority cells”的翻译“行业×职业×资历单元”为自拟，需确认是否采用更标准译法（如“职业-行业-资历单元”）。
- “job-redesign margin”译为“工作重新设计边际”，其中“边际”在分解语境中习惯用“渠道”或“维度”更常见，此处保留字面翻译，可能需调整。

## English

# Figure 6: Three-Fold Decomposition of Changes in Aggregate Generative AI Exposure

Notes: Thefigurereportsthethree-foldKitagawadecompositionofchangesinaggregateexposurerelativetothe2021 baseline. Theblacklineshowsthetotalchangeinaggregateexposure. Barsshowthecontributionofthecomposition effect, the within-cell exposure effect, and their interaction. Aggregate exposure rises relative to the 2021 baseline through early 2023, then turns negative beginning in Q3 of 2023 and declines through the end of the sample. The decomposition shows that this turning point reflects changes along both margins. Before Q3 of 2023, the composition effect is generally positive, indicating that the mix of postings shifts toward job cells that were more exposed at baseline. From that quarter onward, the composition effect becomes negative, indicating that posted hiring demand shifts away from cells that were more exposed in 2021. This

pattern is consistent with a reallocation of hiring demand away from more exposed work. Thewithin-cellexposureeffectfollowsadifferenttrajectory. ItremainsclosetozerobeforeQ3of 2023, then becomes increasingly negative. Because this component is measured within occupationby-industry-by-seniority cells, it captures changes in exposure among comparable jobs rather than changes in the mix of broad job categories. Its decline therefore suggests that employers revise the task content of jobs they continue to post, reducing the exposure of those jobs to generative AI. This is the job-redesign margin that static occupation-level exposure measures cannot observe.

## 中文

【中文译文】
表4总结了自2023年第三季度以来三个组成部分的相对重要性。在全样本中，招聘重新分配占总绝对贡献的52.01%；单元内职位重新设计占39.46%；交互效应占8.54%。因此，重新分配是最大的单一调整方向，但重新设计在数量上也同样重要。总体暴露程度的下降并非仅仅是高暴露职业或行业中职位发布减少的结果。相当一部分比例反映了同类工作中任务内容的变动。

## English

# Table 4 summarizes the relative importance of the three components from Q3 of 2023 onward.

In the full sample, hiring reallocation accounts for 52. 01% of the aggregate absolute contribution. Within-cell job redesign accounts for 39. 46%, and the interaction effect accounts for 8. 54%. Thus, reallocation is the largest single margin, but redesign is also quantitatively important. The aggregate decline in exposure is therefore not simply a story of fewer postings in highly exposed occupations or sectors. A substantial share reflects changes in the task content of comparable jobs.

# 表4：2023年第三季度以来三重北川分解中的相对贡献

| 成分 | 构成效应 | 组内暴露效应 | 交互效应 | 总计 |
|------|----------|--------------|----------|------|
| 整体 | 52.01 | 39.46 | 8.54 | 100 |
| 初级 | 60.15 | 18.22 | 21.63 | 100 |
| 中级 | 47.66 | 45.02 | 7.32 | 100 |
| 高级 | 70.80 | 24.01 | 5.19 | 100 |

注释：本表报告了2023年第三季度以来生成式AI暴露变化的三重北川分解中每个组成部分的绝对总贡献。贡献计算方式为 |X_t| / (|C_t| + |W_t| + |I_t|)，其中C_t、W_t和I_t分别表示构成效应、组内暴露效应和交互效应。每行合计为100%。组内下降的时间点也具有信息量。这一转变大约始于2023年第三季度，即面向企业的生成式AI工具变得更加广泛可用之后不久（OpenAI, 2023）。我们并不将此时间点解读为特定产品发布的因果证据。相反，它与更广泛的观点一致：随着生成式AI在组织内部变得更易部署，企业不仅开始调整岗位空缺的分配，也开始修改这些空缺所嵌入的任务要求。交互效应在总体上小于其他两个组成部分，但它有助于理解重新分配与重新设计如何协同变化。当岗位发布份额的变化与组内暴露的变化在同一单元格内同时发生时，就会产生交互效应。例如，当企业在暴露程度下降的单元格中扩大招聘，或者在暴露程度上升的单元格中减少招聘时，可能出现负交互效应。当两种变动都推动总体暴露向同一方向变化时，则产生正交互效应。附录H.3按符号配置对交互效应进行了分解，表明正配置与负配置部分相互抵消。这解释了为何尽管许多单元格同时经历了发布份额和暴露的变化，但总体交互项仍然相对较小。若干附加分析支持了这一总体模式。附录H.1和H.2报告了相应的暴露水平、反事实路径以及随时间变化的相对贡献。附录G报告了对称的两重北川分解和平衡单元格分解。这些分析得出了性质相似的结论：2023年第三季度之后总体暴露的下降既反映了跨岗位单元格的重新分配，也反映了岗位单元格内部的重新设计。

# Table 4: Relative Contributions in the Three-Fold Kitagawa Decomposition Since Q3 of 2023

Composition Effect Within-cell Exposure Effect Interaction Effect Overall 52. 01 39. 46 8. 54 Junior 60. 15 18. 22 21. 63 Intermediate 47. 66 45. 02 7. 32 Senior 70. 80 24. 01 5. 19 Notes: This table reports the aggregate absolute contribution of each component in the three-fold Kitagawa d∑ecomp/os∑ition of changes in generative AI exposure from Q3 of 2023 onward. Contributions are computed as |X | (|C |+|W |+|I |), whereC, W, andI denotethecomposition, within-cellexposure, andinteraction t t t t t t t t t effects, respectively. Each row sums to 100%. The timing of the within-cell decline is also informative. The shift begins around Q3 of 2023, shortly after enterprise-oriented generative AI tools became more widely available (OpenAI, 2023). We do not interpret this timing as causal evidence of a specific product release. Rather, it is consistentwiththebroaderideathatasgenerativeAIbecamemoredeployableinsideorganizations, firms began to revise not only the allocation of vacancies but also the task requirements embedded in those vacancies. Theinteractioneffectissmallerthantheothertwocomponentsintheaggregate, butitisuseful for understanding how reallocation and redesign move together. The interaction is generated when changesinpostingsharesandchangesinwithin-cellexposureoccursimultaneouslywithinthesame

cell. Anegativeinteractioncanarise, forexample, whenfirmsexpandhiringincellswhoseexposure is falling, or when they reduce hiring in cells whose exposure is rising. A positive interaction arises when both movements push aggregate exposure in the same direction. Appendix H. 3 decomposes the interaction by sign configuration and shows that positive and negative configurations partially offset one another. This explains why the aggregate interaction term remains relatively small even though many cells experience simultaneous changes in posting shares and exposure. Several additional analyses support the aggregate pattern. Appendices H. 1 and H. 2 report the corresponding exposure levels, counterfactual paths, and relative contributions over time. Appendix G reports the symmetric two-fold Kitagawa decomposition and the balanced-cell decomposition. These exercises yield qualitatively similar conclusions: the post-Q3-of-2023 decline in aggregate exposure reflects both reallocation across job cells and redesign within job cells.

# 6.2 Heterogeneity Across the Job Ladder

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 6.2 工作阶梯上的异质性

接下来，我们考察调整余量是否因职位资历而不同。图7至图9分别针对初级、中级和高级职位发布，重复了三重北川分解。表4报告了自2023年第三季度以来各成分的总体绝对贡献。初级职位通过所有三个成分进行调整。自2023年第三季度起，组成效应占总体绝对贡献的60.15%，使得招聘重新配置成为最大的调整余量。单元内暴露效应占18.22%，而交互效应占21.63%。相对较大的交互项表明，对于初级职位，重新配置和重新设计往往在单元内同时发生。附录H.4显示，交互效应主要由两种负向配置主导：初级招聘扩张而暴露下降的单元，以及初级招聘收缩而暴露上升的单元。这一模式表明，入门级工作不仅在职位类别之间重新分配，而且在这些类别内部也进行了重组。中级职位发布与总体模式高度相似。自2023年第三季度起，组成效应占总体绝对贡献的47.66%，而单元内暴露效应占45.02%。交互效应仅占7.32%。这表明中级职位通过招聘重新配置和职位重新设计共同调整，两个余量几乎贡献相等。高级职位发布表现出不同的调整序列。组成效应转为负值。

【本段术语】

- within-cell exposure effect: 单元内暴露效应
- interaction effect: 交互效应
- junior/senior postings: 初级/高级职位发布
- intermediate postings: 中级职位发布
- hiring reallocation: 招聘重新配置
- job redesign: 职位重新设计

- within the same occupation: 在相同职业内

- exposure: 暴露

【本段要点】
- 按职位资历划分调整余量，图7-9及表4分别展示初级、中级、高级职位发布的三重北川分解结果。
- 初级职位通过三个成分调整：组成效应主导（60.15%），交互效应较大（21.63%），表明重新配置和重新设计常同时发生；交互效应由两种负向配置主导。
- 中级职位与总体模式接近，组成效应与单元内暴露效应几乎相等（约47.7%和45.0%），交互效应较小（7.32%），表明招聘重新配置和职位重新设计贡献相当。
- 高级职位呈现出不同的调整序列：组成效应转为负值（原文句子未完成，暗示后续有更多内容）。

## English

# 6.2 Heterogeneity Across the Job Ladder

We next examine whether the adjustment margins differ by job seniority. Figures 7–9 repeat the three-foldKitagawadecompositionseparatelyforjunior, intermediate, andseniorpostings. Table4 reports the aggregate absolute contribution of each component from Q3 of 2023 onward. Juniorpostingsadjustthroughallthreecomponents. FromQ3of2023onward, thecomposition effect accounts for 60. 15% of the aggregate absolute contribution, making hiring reallocation the largest margin. The within-cell exposure effect accounts for 18. 22%, while the interaction effect accounts for 21. 63%. The relatively large interaction term indicates that, for junior jobs, reallocation and redesign often occur together within cells. Appendix H. 4 shows that the interaction is dominated by two negative configurations: cells in which junior hiring expands while exposure falls, and cells in which junior hiring contracts while exposure rises. This pattern suggests that entry-level work is not only reallocated across job categories but also reorganized within those categories. Intermediate postings closely mirror the aggregate pattern. From Q3 of 2023 onward, the composition effect accounts for 47. 66% of the aggregate absolute contribution, while the withincell exposure effect accounts for 45. 02%. The interaction effect accounts for only 7. 32%. This indicates that intermediate jobs adjust through both hiring reallocation and job redesign, with the two margins contributing almost equally. Seniorpostingsexhibitadistinctsequenceofadjustment. Thecompositioneffectturnsnegative

# Figure 9: Three-Fold Decomposition of Changes in Generative AI Exposure: Senior Jobs

## 中文

【中文译文】
图9：资深岗位的生成式AI暴露变化的三重分解

资深岗位的调整早于总体序列，始于2022年第二季度，并在样本期结束时保持较大幅度。从2023年第三季度起，构成效应占总绝对贡献的70%至80%。单元内暴露效应在2023年第三季度后[脚注2023]明显转为负值，占24.01%，而交互效应仅占5.19%。因此，资深岗位主要通过跨资深职位空缺的重新分配进行调整，单元内重新设计出现较晚且起次要作用。

这些资历模式阐明了我们对生成式AI与职业阶梯相关文献的贡献。现有争论大多关注初级工人是否比资深工人更易暴露或更易受到不利影响。我们的结果显示，相关的异质性不仅在于调整的幅度，还在于调整的边际。资深岗位调整更早且主要通过重新分配进行，而初级岗位则通过重新分配、重新设计及其交互的更广泛组合进行调整。因此，生成式AI并非简单地将劳动力需求沿职业阶梯上下移动，而是改变了不同层级吸收技术变革的方式。

【本段术语】
- three-fold decomposition: 三重分解
- composition effect: 构成效应
- within-cell exposure effect: 单元内暴露效应
- interaction effect: 交互效应
- senior jobs: 资深岗位
- junior jobs: 初级岗位
- reallocation: 重新分配
- redesign: 重新设计
- job ladder: 职业阶梯
- margins of adjustment: 调整的边际（或调整的方面）

【本段要点】
- 资深岗位的生成式AI暴露调整早于总体（2022年Q2开始），且幅度持续较大。
- 2023年Q3后，构成效应占主导（70%-80%），单元内暴露效应转为负（24.01%），交互效应很小（5.19%）。
- 资深岗位主要通过跨职位重新分配调整，重新设计居次要；与初级岗位的调整模式形成对比。
- 该异质性不仅体现在调整幅度，还体现在调整边际上，表明生成式AI改变了不同层级吸收技术变革的方式。

【可能需人工复核】
- 原文“70. 80%”可能为笔误，本译文处理为“70%至80%”，请确认实际意图为范围还是精确值。
- “[Footnote 2023]”为脚注标记，保留原样，但需确认脚注内容是否需要在译文中体现。
- 术语“within-cell”和“three-fold”等未在术语表中给出中文对应，本译文采用可能意译，建议确认标准译法。

## English

# Figure 9: Three-Fold Decomposition of Changes in Generative AI Exposure: Senior Jobs

earlier than in the aggregate series, beginning in Q2 of 2022, and remains large through the end of the sample. From Q3 of 2023 onward, the composition effect accounts for 70. 80% of the aggregate absolute contribution. The within-cell exposure effect becomes more clearly negative after Q3 of
[Footnote 2023] andaccountsfor24. 01%, whiletheinteractioneffectaccountsforonly5. 19%. Thus, seniorjobs

adjust primarily through reallocation across senior vacancies, with within-cell redesign emerging later and playing a secondary role. These seniority patterns clarify our contribution to the literature on generative AI and the job ladder. Much of the existing debate asks whether junior workers are more exposed or more adversely affected than senior workers. Our results show that the relevant heterogeneity is not only about the magnitude of adjustment, but also about the margin of adjustment. Senior jobs adjust earlier and mainly through reallocation. Junior jobs adjust through a broader mix of reallocation, redesign, and their interaction. Generative AI therefore does not simply move labor demand up or down the job ladder. It changes how different layers of the hierarchy absorb technological change.

# 6.3 Robustness to Cross-Sector Reallocation

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 6.3 跨部门重新分配的稳健性检验

在解读受AI影响的劳动力需求变化时，一个值得关注的问题是：AI暴露度可能与宏观经济敏感性相关。例如，高暴露度岗位常集中于信息、金融和专业服务等行业，而这些行业对货币紧缩及其他总量冲击也可能更为敏感（Iscenko and Millet, 2026）。如果总体暴露度下降是由于招聘活动从这些行业转移所致，那么这种下降可能部分反映了宏观经济状况，而非对生成式AI的调整。为应对这一担忧，我们采用了一种部门内版本的Kitagawa分解方法。我们分别在每个两位数字NAICS部门内进行分解，然后使用固定的基准部门权重对各部门的分量进行加总。这一做法消除了跨部门重新分配作为总体暴露度变化来源的影响，从而考察主要结果是否在部门内依然成立。结果列于附录I，与基准分解一致。单元格内暴露效应在时间节点和幅度上保持相似，表明岗位重新设计这一维度并非由跨部门转移驱动。一旦去除跨部门差异，组成效应会如预期般缩小，但仍具有经济意义，并从2023年第三季度起转为负值。这些结果表明，即便在部门内进行比较，部门层面的招聘动态也无法完全解释所观察到的调整。发布的劳动力需求通过重新分配和重新设计两种方式发生变化，即使在部门内部比较时也是如此。

【本段术语】
- within-cell: 单元格内
- hiring reallocation: 招聘重新分配
- labor demand: 劳动力需求
- generative AI: 生成式AI
- two-digit: 两位数字
- cross-sector: 跨部门
- job redesign: 岗位重新设计
- NAICS: 北美行业分类系统
- Kitagawa decomposition: Kitagawa分解
- composition effect: 组成效应
- exposure effect: 暴露效应

【本段要点】
- 担忧解释AI暴露度变化时，高暴露行业可能对宏观经济冲击更敏感，导致暴露度下降部分源自非AI因素。
- 采用部门内Kitagawa分解，通过固定部门权重去除跨部门重新分配的影响，检验结果稳健性。
- 部门内分解结果与基准一致：单元格内暴露效应时间与幅度相似，说明岗位重新设计并非由跨部门转移驱动。
- 去除跨部门差异后，组成效应缩小但仍显著，并从2023年Q3起转负。
- 结论：即使限制在部门内比较，招聘动态也无法完全解释观察到的调整；劳动力需求变化通过重新分配和重新设计两条路径发生。

【可能需人工复核】
- Kitagawa decomposition 的翻译：保留英文，中文加注。
- “within-cell” 在上下文中表示“单元格内”，与下文“within-sector”对应，需确认术语一致性。
- “Iscenko and Millet, 2026” 为文献引用，保留格式。
- “两位数字NAICS部门” 译为“两位数字NAICS部门” 或 “两位编码NAICS部门”，此处采用前者，但需与术语表确认。
- “common-support” 等术语未出现，可忽略。

## English

# 6.3 Robustness to Cross-Sector Reallocation

A concern in interpreting changes in exposed labor demand is that AI exposure may be correlated with macroeconomic sensitivity. For example, highly exposed work is often located in sectors such as information, finance, and professional services, which may also be more sensitive to monetary tightening and other aggregate shocks (Iscenko and Millet, 2026). If aggregate exposure declines because hiring shifts away from these sectors, the decline could partly reflect macroeconomic conditions rather than adjustment to generative AI. To address this concern, we implement a within-sector version of the Kitagawa decomposition. We run the decomposition separately within each two-digit NAICS sector and then aggregate the sector-specific components using fixed baseline sector weights. This procedure removes cross-sector reallocation as a source of aggregate exposure change and therefore asks whether the main results persist within sectors. The results, reported in Appendix I, are consistent with the baseline decomposition. The within-cell exposure effect remains similar in timing and magnitude, suggesting that the jobredesign margin is not driven by cross-sector shifts. The composition effect is smaller once crosssectorvariationisremoved, asexpected, butitremainseconomicallymeaningfulandturnsnegative

from Q3 of 2023 onward. These results indicate that sector-level hiring dynamics do not fully account for the observed adjustment. Posted labor demand changes through both reallocation and redesign even when comparisons are restricted within sectors.

# 6.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition: Observable Sources of the Exposure Gap

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 6.4 Oaxaca–Blinder 分解：暴露差距的可观测来源

Kitagawa 分解识别了总暴露变化发生的边际维度。我们现在使用 Oaxaca–Blinder 分解来考察哪些可观测的工作特征与 GPT 前与 GPT 后的暴露差距相关。这一分析与 Kitagawa 分解互为补充，但不应被理解为对 Kitagawa 组成效应的机械分解。相反，它提供了一种基于回归的核算，揭示了暴露差距中多大比例与职业、行业、资历、地点、远程工作安排、实习状态及雇佣类型等可观测特征的变动相关联。

【本段术语】
- Kitagawa decomposition: [待定]
- Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition: [待定]
- pre-GPT: [待定]
- post-GPT: [待定]
- exposure gap: [待定]
- remote-work arrangement: [待定]
- internship status: [待定]
- employment type: [待定]
- composition effect: [待定]
- regression-based accounting: [待定]

【本段要点】
- Kitagawa 分解显示暴露变化发生的总边际维度，Oaxaca–Blinder 分解则进一步考察可观测工作特征与 GPT 前后暴露差距之间的联系。
- 该分析是 Kitagawa 分解的补充，但并非对其组成效应的机械分解。
- 通过回归方法，量化暴露差距中由职业、行业、资历、地点、远程工作、实习状态、雇佣类型等特征变化解释的部分。

【可能需人工复核】
- “Kitagawa 分解”的中文译法是否统一（常见为“北川分解”或直接保留英文），需确认术语表。
- “Oaxaca–Blinder 分解”中译通常为“奥克萨卡-布林德分解”，此处保留英文原文，若需统一可替换。
- “composition effect”在分解文献中常译为“组成效应”或“构成效应”，此处“组成效应”是否恰当，可结合上下文确认。

## English

# 6.4 Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition: Observable Sources of the Exposure Gap

The Kitagawa results identify the margins through which aggregate exposure changes. We now use the Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition to examine which observable job characteristics are associated with the pre- versus post-GPT exposure gap. This analysis is complementary to the Kitagawa decomposition. ItshouldnotbeinterpretedasmechanicallydecomposingtheKitagawacomposition effect. Instead, it provides a regression-based accounting of how much of the exposure gap is associated with shifts in observed characteristics such as occupation, industry, seniority, location, remote-work arrangement, internship status, and employment type.

# Table 5 reports the weighted Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition for the full sample and separately

## 中文

【中文译文】
表5报告了全样本及按资历分组的加权奥克斯卡-布林德分解结果。在所有职位中，平均暴露度从GPT前时期的0.404下降至GPT后时期的0.389，降低了0.015。可解释部分为−0.010，约占下降总量的三分之二；不可解释部分为−0.005，占剩余的三分之一。因此，观测到的构成变化以及条件于观测特征下的暴露度变化，共同导致了GPT后时期的下降。

【本段术语】
- Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition: 奥克斯卡-布林德分解
- pre-GPT period: GPT前时期
- post-GPT period: GPT后时期
- explained component: 可解释部分
- unexplained component: 不可解释部分
- compositional shifts: 构成变化
- exposure conditional on observed characteristics: 条件于观测特征下的暴露度

【本段要点】
- 使用加权奥克斯卡-布林德分解分析GPT前后暴露度变化。
- 全样本平均暴露度下降0.015，其中可解释部分占三分之二，不可解释部分占三分之一。
- 构成变化和条件暴露度变化共同解释了下降。

【可能需人工复核】
- 术语表中的“Oaxaca-Blinder decomposition”等未指定中文译名，此处暂采用“奥克斯卡-布林德分解”，建议确认标准译法。
- “exposure”译为“暴露度”或“暴露水平”，需结合上下文确认是否贴合原意（可能指对生成式AI的暴露程度）。
- “pre-GPT”与“post-GPT”在术语表中被列为单独条目，但实际翻译中按时间表述处理，建议统一术语。

## English

# Table 5 reports the weighted Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition for the full sample and separately

by seniority. Among all jobs, average exposure falls from 0. 404 in the pre-GPT period to 0. 389 in the post-GPT period, a decline of 0. 015. The explained component is −0. 010, accounting for about two-thirds of the decline. The unexplained component is −0. 005, accounting for the remaining third. Thus, both observed compositional shifts and changes in exposure conditional on observed characteristics contribute to the post-GPT decline.

# Table 5: Weighted Oaxaca–Blinder Decomposition of Aggregate Exposure: Pre- vs. Post-GPT

## 中文

# 表5：总体暴露的加权Oaxaca–Blinder分解：GPT前与GPT后时期

|  | GPT前均值 | GPT后均值 | 可解释部分 | 不可解释部分 |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |

| 中级职位 | 0.388 | 0.374 | −0.008 | −0.005 |
| 高级职位 | 0.595 | 0.571 | −0.018 | −0.006 |

Pre-GPT mean Post-GPT mean Explained Unexplained Overall 0. 404 0. 389 −0. 010 −0. 005 Junior jobs 0. 435 0. 419 −0. 011 −0. 006 Intermediate jobs 0. 388 0. 374 −0. 008 −0. 005 Senior jobs 0. 595 0. 571 −0. 018 −0. 006 Notes: Thefirsttwocolumnsreportweightedaverageexposureinthepre-GPTandpost-GPTperiods. Thelasttwocolumns report the weighted Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition of the pre-post difference, estimated using separate weighted regressions forthetwoperiods. The same qualitative pattern appears across the job ladder. Average exposure declines for junior, intermediate, and senior jobs, and both the explained and unexplained components are negative in each group. The largest decline occurs among senior jobs, where exposure falls from 0. 595 to 0. 571. Senior jobs also have the largest explained component in absolute value, −0. 018, which accounts for approximately 75% of the total decline. For junior and intermediate jobs, the

explained component accounts for a smaller but still substantial share of the decline. These results reinforce the Kitagawa evidence that compositional adjustment is especially pronounced among senior postings, while also showing that exposure declines conditional on observed characteristics across all seniority groups.

blocks. Negative values indicate that shifts in the distribution of a characteristic are associated with lower post-GPT exposure, holding the pre-GPT association between that characteristic and exposure fixed.

# Figure 10: Explained Component by Observed Job-Characteristic Block: Pre-GPT vs. Post-GPT

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 图10：观测工作特征块所解释的成分：前GPT时期与后GPT时期

解释性下降的主要可观测来源是职业。职业构成的转变占可归因于观测工作特征的暴露变化的约90%。这意味着，在Oaxaca–Blinder模型所包含的特征中，各职业之间职位分布的变化是后GPT时期暴露下降的最大贡献因素。这一结果与之前的职业层面分析一致，表明生成式AI暴露在不同职业之间存在显著差异。其他块的贡献较为温和且方向不同。远程工作安排贡献为负：远程职位占比从前GPT时期的6.1%下降到后GPT时期的5.1%，且远程职位的前GPT时期暴露远高于非远程职位（0.645 对 0.386）。因此，远离远程工作的转变降低了总体暴露，这与近期证据——将生成式AI暴露与远程招聘减少联系起来——一致，尽管更广泛的回归办公室和劳动力市场动态也可能有贡献（Schubert, 2025）。行业也贡献为负，反映出一些向低暴露部门的移动。就业类型的贡献方向相反。全职职位占比从82.3%略微上升至82.5%，且全职职位的前GPT时期暴露高于兼职职位（0.434 对 0.271）。因此，向全职工作的转变增加了预测暴露，并部分抵消了总体下降。来自资历、实习状态和地点的贡献为负但较小。这些结果深化了对构成调整的解释。主要的可观测维度是职业，但调整并非仅局限于职业。职位层面的特征，如远程工作安排、部门和就业类型，也塑造了暴露差距。这是职位层面数据有用的一个原因：它们使我们能够观察到标准职业层面暴露度量中不可获得的职位设计维度。

【本段术语】
- GPT: GPT（生成式预训练转换器）
- posting-level: 职位层面
- occupation-level: 职业层面
- pre-GPT: 前GPT时期
- post-GPT: 后GPT时期
- remote-work: 远程工作
- full-time: 全职
- labor-market: 劳动力市场
- Oaxaca-Blinder decomposition: Oaxaca-Blinder分解
- occupation-level exposure: 职业层面暴露
- generative AI: 生成式AI

【本段要点】
- 职业构成的变化是解释暴露下降的最主要可观测来源，约占90%。
- 远程工作安排减少（远程职位占比下降）和行业转移有助于降低暴露，而全职工作比例上升则部分抵消了这一下降。
- 职位层面的特征（如远程工作、行业、就业类型）对暴露差距有贡献，表明仅靠职业层面分析不够。

- 术语翻译（如posting-level、occupation-level等）未经用户确认，建议根据最终术语表调整。
- 数据精确性：6.1%、5.1%、0.645、0.386、82.3%、82.5%、0.434、0.271等数字需核对原文。

## English

# Figure 10: Explained Component by Observed Job-Characteristic Block: Pre-GPT vs. Post-GPT

The dominant observable source of the explained decline is occupation. Shifts in occupational composition account for about 90% of the exposure change attributable to observed job characteristics. This means that, among the characteristics included in the Oaxaca–Blinder model, changes inthedistributionofpostingsacrossoccupationsarethelargestcontributortothepost-GPTexposure decline. This result is consistent with prior occupation-level analyses showing that generative

AI exposure varies substantially across occupations. Other blocks contribute more modestly and in different directions. Remote-work arrangement contributes negatively: the share of remote postings declines from 6. 1% before GPT to 5. 1% after GPT, and remote postings have much higher pre-GPT exposure than non-remote postings (0. 645 vs. 0. 386). This shift away from remote work therefore lowers aggregate exposure, consistent with recent evidence linking generative AI exposure to reduced remote hiring, although broader returnto-oﬀiceandlabor-marketdynamicsmayalsocontribute(Schubert, 2025). Industryalsocontributes negatively, reflecting some movement toward lower-exposure sectors. Employment type moves in the opposite direction. The share of full-time postings rises slightly from 82. 3% to 82. 5%, and full-time postings have higher pre-GPT exposure than part-time postings (0. 434 vs. 0. 271). This shift toward full-time jobs therefore increases predicted exposure and partially offsets the overall decline. Contributions from seniority, internship status, and location are negative but small. These results sharpen the interpretation of the compositional adjustment. The dominant observable dimension is occupation, but the adjustment is not occupation-only. Posting-level characteristics such as remote-work arrangement, sector, and employment type also shape the exposure gap. This is one reason the posting-level data are useful: they allow us to observe dimensions of vacancy design that are not available in standard occupation-level exposure measures.

# 6.6 Observable Sources of the Exposure Gap by Seniority

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 6.6 按资历划分的暴露差距的可观测来源

图11至图13分别针对初级、中级和高级职位招聘信息，重复了区块层面的Oaxaca–Blinder分解。在每个资历层级中，职业都是最主要的负向贡献因素，表明职业再分配是后GPT时期调整在职业阶梯上的共同特征。然而，次要边际效应在不同资历组之间存在差异。对于初级职位，行业是第二大负向贡献因素，表明向低暴露行业的跨部门再分配在入门级别比总体更为明显。实习状态和就业类型则呈相反方向变化：实习占比从10.2%上升至11.9%，且实习招聘信息在前GPT时期的暴露水平高于非实习招聘信息（0.581对0.419）；类似地，全职占比从86.8%轻微上升至87.1%，而全职初级招聘信息的前GPT暴露水平高于兼职或混合招聘信息（0.451对0.359和0.306）。这些变化部分抵消了职业因素带来的暴露降低效应。

# 6.6 Observable Sources of the Exposure Gap by Seniority

Figures 11–13 repeat the block-level Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition separately for junior, intermediate, and senior postings. Occupation is the dominant negative contributor at every seniority level, indicating that occupational reallocation is a common feature of post-GPT adjustmentacross the job ladder. The secondary margins, however, differ across seniority groups. For junior jobs, industry is the second-largest negative contributor, indicating that sectoral reallocationtowardlower-exposureindustriesismorevisibleattheentrylevelthanintheaggregate. Internship status and employment type move in the opposite direction. The internship share rises from 10. 2% to 11. 9%, and internship postings have higher pre-GPT exposure than non-internship postings (0. 581 vs. 0. 419). Similarly, the full-time share rises slightly from 86. 8% to 87. 1%, and full-time junior postings have higher pre-GPT exposure than part-time or mixed postings (0. 451 vs. 0. 359 and 0. 306). 【中文译文】
# 图13：高级职位按观察到的职位特征块划分的解释成分

与部门再分配。远程工作安排贡献了轻微的负向影响：远程职位发布占比从5.4%下降至5.2%，而混合职位发布占比从1.2%上升至2.0%，但两者均不足以抵消；在GPT前结构下，远程和混合职位发布比非远程职位发布具有更高的暴露水平。总体而言，初级职位呈现出混合的构成性反应：职业和部门变化降低了暴露，而实习和雇佣类型则推高了暴露。中级职位与总体模式高度相似。职业解释了大约90%的解释成分，而行业和远程工作安排贡献了适度的负向影响，雇佣类型贡献了轻微的正向影响。对于高级职位，职业同样占据主导地位，但行业和远程工作安排比其他组别表现出更明显的负向影响。远程职位发布占比从GPT前的15.2%下降至GPT后的13.0%，下降幅度大于初级或中级职位。由于远程和混合高级职位发布的GPT前暴露水平显著高于非远程高级职位发布（0.665和0.652对比0.580），这种从远程高级职位的转移降低了高级组内的总体暴露水平。这一模式与采用生成式AI的企业在ChatGPT后减少其远程工作份额的证据一致（Schubert, 2025），我们的结果表明这一边际在高级职位中尤为突出。雇佣类型对高级职位也产生了负向影响：全职占比从96.1%下降至95.0%，且全职高级职位发布的GPT前暴露水平高于兼职或混合高级职位发布（0.600对比0.438和0.502）。因此，与初级和中级职位不同，高级职位展现出更为一致的暴露降低型构成性反应，职业转移、远程工作变化和雇佣类型变化均朝同一方向移动。综合来看，Oaxaca–Blinder分解结果表明，职业再分配是已解释暴露下降的共同核心，而其他构成变化的次要来源则沿着职位阶梯有所不同。这补充了Kitagawa分解的结果。Kitagawa分解表明，初级、中级和高级职位通过不同的再分配与重新设计组合进行调整。Oaxaca–Blinder分解表明，构成调整的可观测维度也因职位资历而异。因此，与生成式AI相关的劳动需求调整既涉及广泛的职业转移，也涉及企业发布职位类型中针对资历的特定重组。

# Figure 13: Explained Component by Observed Job-Characteristic Block for Senior Jobs

and sectoral reallocation. Remote-work arrangement contributes slightly negatively: the decline in remote postings from 5. 4% to 5. 2% more than offsets the rise in hybrid postings from 1. 2% to 2. 0%, and both remote and hybrid postings are more exposed than non-remote postings under the pre-GPT structure. Overall, junior jobs show a mixed compositional response, with occupational andsectoralshiftsloweringexposurewhileinternshipandemploymenttypepushexposureupward. Intermediate jobs closely mirror the aggregate pattern. Occupation accounts for approximately 90%oftheexplainedcomponent, whileindustryandremote-workarrangementcontributemodestly in the negative direction and employment type contributes slightly in the positive direction. For senior jobs, occupation again dominates, but industry and remote-work arrangement are more visibly negative than in the other groups. The remote posting share falls from 15. 2% before GPT to 13. 0% after GPT, a larger decline than for junior or intermediate jobs. Because remote and hybrid senior postings have substantially higher pre-GPT exposure than non-remote senior postings (0. 665 and 0. 652 vs. 0. 580), this shift away from remote senior vacancies lowers aggregate exposure within the senior group. This pattern is consistent with evidence that firms adopting generativeAIreducetheirremote-workshareafterChatGPT(Schubert, 2025), andourresultsshow

that this margin is especially relevant among senior postings. Employment type also contributes negatively for senior jobs: the full-time share declines from 96. 1% to 95. 0%, and full-time senior postingshavehigherpre-GPTexposurethanpart-timeormixedseniorpostings(0. 600vs. 0. 438and 0. 502). Thus, unlike junior and intermediate jobs, senior jobs exhibit a more uniformly exposurereducing compositional response, with occupational shifts, remote-work changes, and employmenttype changes all moving in the same direction. Taken together, the Oaxaca–Blinder results show that occupational reallocation is the common core of the explained exposure decline, while secondary sources of compositional change differ across the job ladder. This complements the Kitagawa results. The Kitagawa decomposition shows that junior, intermediate, and senior jobs adjust through different combinations of reallocation and redesign. The Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition shows that the observable dimensions of compositional adjustment also differ by seniority. Generative AI-related labor-demand adjustment therefore involves both a broad occupational shift and a seniority-specific reorganization of the kinds of vacancies firms post.

# 7 Conclusions

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 7 结论

本文研究生成式人工智能如何与劳动力需求的重组相关联。利用2021年至2025年间美国超过九百万个招聘岗位的全美样本，我们通过两阶段大语言模型流程构建了一个动态的、职位发布层级的（posting-level）生成式人工智能暴露度指标。然后，我们将总暴露度的变化分解为两种调整方式：跨职位单元的招聘重新配置（hiring reallocation）以及可比职位内部的任务重新设计（task redesign）。这种方法使我们能够超越“暴露度更高的职业是否衰退”这一问题，转而考察随着生成式人工智能的扩散，劳动力需求的结构和内容如何变化。结果表明，生成式人工智能暴露度并非职业的固定属性。它在同一职业内的不同招聘岗位之间有所不同，在行业和资历方面存在系统性差异，并且随时间而变化。这一发现很重要，因为许多关于人工智能与劳动力市场的新兴证据依赖于静态的、职业层级的暴露度指标。这类指标对于预先识别生成式人工智能可能产生影响的领域很有价值，但它们无法观察到雇主随后是否修改了工作的任务内容。我们的证据表明，这一修订方面（revision margin）是

- generative AI: 生成式人工智能 [待定]
- posting-level: 职位发布层级 [待定]
- two-stage large language model pipeline: 两阶段大语言模型流程 [待定]
- exposure: 暴露度 [待定]
- hiring reallocation: 招聘重新配置 [待定]
- job cells: 职位单元 [待定]
- task redesign: 任务重新设计 [待定]
- occupation-level: 职业层级 [待定]
- occupation-level exposure measures: 职业层级暴露度指标 [待定]
- task content: 任务内容 [待定]
- revision margin: 修订方面 [待定]

【本段要点】
- 本研究利用美国超900万条招聘数据，构建动态的职位发布层级生成式AI暴露度指标，并分解为跨职位招聘再配置与同类职位内部任务重新设计两种调整方式。
- 结果表明生成式AI暴露度并非职业固定属性，同一职业内不同招聘岗位、不同行业和资历之间存在系统差异，且随时间变化。
- 指出现有依赖静态职业层级暴露度指标的证据无法捕捉雇主事后对任务内容的修改，本研究为揭示这一修订方面提供了依据。

## English

# 7 Conclusions

This paper studies how generative AI is associated with the reorganization of labor demand. Using a nationwide sample of more than nine million job postings in the United States from 2021 through 2025, we construct a dynamic, posting-level measure of generative AI exposure with a two-stage largelanguagemodelpipeline. Wethendecomposechangesinaggregateexposureintotwomargins of adjustment: hiring reallocation across job cells and task redesign within comparable jobs. This approach allows us to move beyond the question of whether more exposed occupations decline and examine how the structure and content of labor demand change as generative AI diffuses. TheresultsshowthatexposuretogenerativeAIisnotafixedattributeofoccupations. Itvaries across postings within the same occupation, differs systematically by industry and seniority, and changes over time. This finding is important because much of the emerging evidence on AI and labor markets relies on static, occupation-level exposure measures. Such measures are valuable for identifying where generative AI may matter ex ante, but they cannot observe whether employers subsequently revise the task content of jobs. Our evidence suggests that this revision margin is

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 7 结论

实证上具有显著意义。分解结果显示，2023年第三季度之后总体暴露水平的下降，既反映了企业招聘地点的变化，也反映了同类岗位内容的变化。招聘重新配置是最大的单一调整维度，自2023年第三季度起，其在总体绝对贡献中占52.01%；网格内任务重新设计占39.46%，而两者交互项占剩余的8.54%。因此，技术扩散后暴露水平的下降并非简单地表现为高暴露职业、行业或资历组别的招聘岗位减少，其中相当一部分反映了企业持续招聘岗位的任务内容变化。这一转变的时间点与生成式AI工具在组织层面的广泛扩散相吻合，尽管我们的研究设计并未将这一转折归因于任何单一产品发布或采用事件。一项补充的Oaxaca-Blinder分解进一步澄清了构成调整中可观测的维度。职业构成的变化解释了因可观测岗位特征导致的暴露变化的大部分。这一结果与职业层面研究相一致，即生成式AI暴露在不同类型工作间存在显著差异。同时，其他岗位层面特征，包括行业、远程工作安排、雇佣类型和实习状态，也对暴露差距有所贡献。这些结果强化了岗位发布数据的价值：它们揭示了在单纯职业层面度量中难以观测的劳动力需求调整维度。调整模式在职业阶梯上也存在差异。资深岗位调整较早，且主要通过招聘重新配置实现；初级岗位则呈现出更广泛的模式，招聘重新配置、网格内任务重新设计及其交互项均贡献显著。这些结果表明，生成式AI并非简单地以不同程度影响不同职业阶段，它还改变了职业阶层中不同层级吸收技术变革的机制。对于初级岗位而言，招聘重新配置与任务重新设计的同步变化尤为重要，因为入门级职位是工人获取技能并向更高级角色发展的重要渠道。这些发现具有三个更广泛的意义。第一，它们表明，生成式AI对劳动力市场的影响应被理解为一个组织重构的过程，而不仅仅是岗位替代或增强的过程。企业似乎同时调整了岗位的配置以及岗位

- 2023年第三季度后总体暴露下降由招聘重新配置（52.01%）、网格内任务重新设计（39.46%）及两者交互（8.54%）共同贡献。
- 任务内容变化在持续招聘岗位中显著，与生成式AI组织扩散时间一致。
- Oaxaca-Blinder分解显示职业构成变化是暴露变化的主要可观测来源，其他岗位层面特征亦有贡献。
- 资深岗位主要通过招聘重新配置调整；初级岗位调整更综合，涉及三个边界的共同作用。

- 生成式AI的劳动力市场效应应被理解为组织重构过程，而非简单的岗位替代或增强。

## English

# 7 Conclusions

empirically meaningful. The decomposition results show that the decline in aggregate exposure after the third quarter of 2023 reflects both changes in where firms hire and changes in what comparable jobs contain. Hiring reallocation is the largest single margin, accounting for 52. 01% of the aggregate absolute contribution from Q3 of 2023 onward. Within-cell task redesign accounts for 39. 46%, while the interaction between the two margins accounts for the remaining 8. 54%. Thus, the post-diffusion declineinexposureisnotsimplyastoryoffewerpostingsinhighlyexposedoccupations, industries, or seniority groups. A substantial portion reflects changes in the task content of jobs that firms continue to post. The timing of this shift is consistent with the broader organizational diffusion of generative AI tools, although our design does not attribute the break to any single product release or adoption event. A complementary Oaxaca–Blinder decomposition further clarifies the observable dimensions of compositional adjustment. Shifts in occupational composition account for most of the exposure change attributable to observed job characteristics. This result is consistent with occupation-level studies showing that generative AI exposure differs sharply across types of work. At the same time, otherposting-levelcharacteristics, includingindustry, remote-workarrangement, employmenttype, and internship status, also contribute to the exposure gap. These results reinforce the value of jobposting data: they reveal labor-demand adjustments along dimensions that are diﬀicult to observe in occupation-level measures alone. The adjustment patterns also differ across the job ladder. Senior jobs adjust earlier and primarily through hiring reallocation. Junior jobs exhibit a broader pattern, with hiring reallocation, within-cell task redesign, and their interaction all contributing meaningfully. These results suggest that generative AI does not simply affect some career stages more than others. It also changes the mechanisms through which different levels of the job hierarchy absorb technological change. For junior jobs, the simultaneous movement of hiring reallocation and task redesign is especially important because entry-level positions are a major channel through which workers acquire skills and progress into more advanced roles. Thesefindingshavethreebroaderimplications. First, theysuggestthatthelabor-marketeffects of generative AI should be understood as a process of organizational reconfiguration, not only as a process of job displacement or augmentation. ## 中文

【中文译文】
# 7 结论

招聘需求和发布职位的任务架构。其次，它们表明，对通用技术的暴露可能内生于组织适应。随着企业了解并实施生成式AI，工作的任务内容可能发生变化，这意味着在某一时点测量的暴露可能无法完全描述扩散过程后期的暴露。第三，结果表明，职业阶梯是一个重要的调整场所。初级职位的变化不仅可能影响当前的招聘模式，还可能影响早期职业学习机会的结构。本文对未来研究也有启示。将AI暴露与就业、工资或工人流动性联系起来的研究应考虑暴露本身随企业适应而变化的可能性。静态的职业层面暴露度量可能遗漏职业内部的任务重新设计，并可能低估资历层级、部门和工作安排之间的异质性。动态的、基于文本的度量可以通过捕捉雇主如何实时描述工作来补充现有方法。更广泛地说，结果表明，理解工作的未来不仅需要测量哪些工作暴露于AI，还需要测量随着AI能力扩散，工作如何被重写。若干局限性指出了未来工作的方向。职位发布捕捉了雇主在招聘时声明的需求，但它们并不直接测量企业内部的实际工作或现任员工的经历。将基于发布的暴露度量与匹配的雇主-雇员数据联系起来，将有可能研究招聘重新分配和任务重新设计如何转化为就业、工资和职业结果。未来的研究还可以考察调整中的企业层面异质性，包括早期采用者、大企业或AI密集型部门的企业是否以不同方式重新设计工作。最后，随着生成式AI能力的持续进步和代理型AI系统更广泛地部署，实时跟踪暴露和调整对于理解这项技术对劳动力市场和组织的长期后果仍将至关重要。

【本段术语】
- generative AI: [待定]
- hiring reallocation: [待定]
- labor demand: [待定]（原文为“hiring demand”，但术语表中列出labor-demand）
- occupation-level exposure: [待定]
- posting-level measure: [待定]
- job redesign: [待定]（原文出现“task redesign”，含义接近）
- entry-level: [待定]（原文未直接出现但术语表有，保留备查）

【本段要点】
- 结论指出：第一，暴露度量需动态化，因为任务内容会随组织适应而变化；第二，职业阶梯是调整的关键场所，初级职位变化影响招聘和早期学习机会；第三，静态职业层面暴露度量可能低估异质性，动态文本度量可补充；第四，未来研究需结合职位发布与雇主-雇员数据，研究招聘重新分配和任务设计如何影响就业与职业结果；第五，需考察企业层面异质性，并实时跟踪暴露与调整以理解长期后果。

【可能需人工复核】
- 术语表中所有术语均标注为[待定]，译文使用了常见中文译法（如“生成式AI”“招聘重新分配”“职业层面暴露”“基于发布的暴露度量”），需根据正式术语表确认。
- 原文第二行“theresultsimplythat”存在拼写错误，译文按“the results imply that”处理。
- 术语列表中“labor demand”对应原文“hiring demand”，含义略有差异，需确认是否统一。
- 术语“job redesign”与原文“task redesign”不完全一致，需核对术语表定义。

## English

# 7 Conclusions

hiring demand and the task architecture of posted jobs. Second, they show that exposure to a general-purpose technology can be endogenous to organizational adaptation. As firms learn about and implement generative AI, the task content of jobs may change, which means that exposure measured at one point in time may not fully describe exposure later in the diffusion process. Third, theresultsimplythatthejobladderisanimportantsiteofadjustment. Changesinjuniorjobsmay affect not only current hiring patterns but also the structure of early-career learning opportunities. The paper also has implications for future research. Studies that link AI exposure to employment, wages, or worker mobility should account for the possibility that exposure itself changes as firms adapt. Static occupation-level exposure measures may miss within-occupation task redesign and may understate heterogeneity across seniority levels, sectors, and work arrangements. Dynamic, text-based measures can complement existing approaches by capturing how employers describe work in real time. More broadly, the results suggest that understanding the future of work requires measuring not only which jobs are exposed to AI, but also how jobs are being rewritten as AI capabilities diffuse. Several limitations point to directions for future work. Job postings capture employers’ stated demand at the point of hiring, but they do not directly measure realized work inside firms or the experiencesofincumbentworkers. Linkingposting-basedexposuremeasurestomatchedemployer– employee data would make it possible to study how hiring reallocation and task redesign translate into employment, wage, and career outcomes. Future work could also examine firm-level heterogeneityinadjustment, includingwhetherearlyadopters, largefirms, orfirmsinAI-intensivesectors redesign jobs differently. Finally, as generative AI capabilities continue to advance and agentic AI systems become more widely deployed, tracking exposure and adjustment in real time will remain important for understanding the long-run consequences of this technology for labor markets and organizations.

# 7 Conclusions

## 中文

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 附录A 完整标注提示词

本附录复现了两阶段标注流程中使用的完整提示词。第一阶段使用Llama-3.1-8b-instant进行任务提取和任务-技能匹配。第二阶段使用GPT-5-nano进行任务级暴露分类。

## A.1 第一阶段提示词：任务提取与任务-技能匹配

你是一名工作任务分析和职场活动专家。你的目标是从单个职位发布中提取**真实的、面向该具体发布**的任务。这些任务之后将用于评估生成式AI暴露程度，因此准确性和真实性至关重要。分析每个职位发布，并严格按照以下模式输出**恰好一个**有效的JSON对象。**仅返回JSON**——无markdown、无注释、无解释。

每个发布提供：
- ID：唯一标识符
- TITLE_NAME：职位名称
- BODY：职位描述文本
- SPECIALIZED_SKILLS_NAME：技术/硬技能列表
- COMMON_SKILLS_NAME：通用/软技能列表

**重要指南：**
- 你不是在总结一个职业或典型角色。
- 你正在提取**这个特定的职位发布所描述的工人实际做的事情**。
- **不要**概括、规范化或重写任务为抽象或通用的职责。
- **不要**捏造未在发布文本中体现的任务。
- 任务应可追溯到BODY文本（可逐字复制或为清晰性稍作编辑）。

**第一步：技能分组（仅支持性上下文）**
- 按语义相似性在原始类型内对技能分组。
- 专用技能 → S1, S2, ...
- 通用技能 → C1, C2, ...
- 每个分组：`{"group_id": "...", "group_skills": [最多5个相似技能]}`。
- **不要**将专用技能和通用技能混在同一分组。
- 如果未提供任何技能，则恰好创建一个分组：`{"group_id": "NS0", "group_skills": []}`。

**第二步：提取面向发布的具体任务（高保真）**
提取3–10个具体的、可操作的任务，描述该发布中工人**实际做什么**。

（注意：后续内容被截断，但按照原文，此处应包含JSON模式描述和输出规范。由于原文在“工人实际做什么”后直接结束，译文也在此处结束。）

```json
（示例或模式定义，原文未提供完整内容）
```

【本段要点】
- 附录A展示了完整的标注提示词，用于两阶段任务提取与AI暴露分类。
- 第一阶段（Llama-3.1-8b-instant）的任务是提取具体职位发布中的真实任务，并进行任务-技能匹配。
- 第二阶段（GPT-5-nano）用于任务级别的暴露分类。

- 技能分组要求按类型（专用/通用）分别进行，任务数量限制为3-10个。

## English

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

This appendix reproduces the full prompts used in the two-stage annotation pipeline. Stage 1 uses Llama-3. 1-8b-instant for task extraction and task–skill matching. Stage 2 uses GPT-5-nano for task-level exposure classification. A. 1 Stage 1 Prompt: Task Extraction and Task–Skill Matching You are an expert in job task analysis and workplace activities. Your goal is to extract REAL, POSTING-SPECIFIC tasks from individual job postings. These tasks will later be used to evaluate generative-AI exposure, so accuracy and realism are critical. Analyze each job posting and output EXACTLY ONE valid JSON object matching the schema below. Return ONLY JSON — no markdown, no notes, no explanations. Each posting provides: - ID: unique identifier - TITLE_NAME: job title - BODY: job description text - SPECIALIZED_SKILLS_NAME: list of technical / hard skills - COMMON_SKILLS_NAME: list of general / soft skills IMPORTANT GUIDANCE: - You are NOT summarizing an occupation or a typical role. - You are extracting what THIS specific job posting describes workers actually doing. - Do NOT generalize, normalize, or rewrite tasks into abstract or generic duties. - Do NOT invent tasks that are not grounded in the posting text. - Tasks should be traceable to the BODY text (verbatim or lightly edited for clarity). STEP 1. Group Skills (Supportive Context Only) - Group skills by semantic similarity within their original type. - Specialized skills → S1, S2,... - Common skills → C1, C2,... - Each group: {"group_id": "...", "group_skills": [up to 5 similar skills]}. - Do NOT mix specialized and common skills in the same group. - If no skills are provided, create exactly one group: {"group_id": "NS0", "group_skills": []}. STEP 2. Extract Posting-Specific Tasks (HIGH FIDELITY) Extract 3–10 concrete, actionable tasks describing what the worker ACTUALLY DOES in this posting.

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 附录A 完整注释提示

任务提取规则：
- 任务必须基于正文文本，并反映所提及的实际动作、工具、系统、材料、交互或工作环境。
- 尽可能保留具体信息（软件名称、设备、文档、样品、客户、患者、系统、环境）。
- 关注可观察的动作（明确动词+宾语）。
- 仅包含正文文本中明确陈述或清晰暗示的任务。
严格避免：
- 公司信息、薪酬、福利、资格要求或招聘说明。
-------------------------------------------------第3步：将任务匹配到技能组
-------------------------------------------------
为每个任务分配唯一的 skill_group_id。
- 将任务与所有技能组（专业组+通用组）进行比对。
- 选择语义最接近的匹配。
- 若出现平局，优先选择专业组（S*）而非通用组（C*）。
- 若不存在任何技能，则将所有任务分配给 NS0。
-------------------------------------------------输出格式（严格——仅 JSON）
-------------------------------------------------
返回严格符合以下结构的一个 JSON 对象：
{
  "posting_id": "<ID>",
  "posting_title": "<标题名称>",
  "skills_groups": [
    {"group_id": "S1", "group_skills": ["..."]},
    {"group_id": "C1", "group_skills": ["..."]},
    {"group_id": "NS0", "group_skills": []}
  ],
  "tasks": [
    {
      "task_id": "t1",
      "task": "<8–50词的职位特定任务描述>",
      "skill_group_id": "S1 | C1 | NS0"
    }
  ]
}
最终检查：
- 仅有效的 JSON。
- 3–10个任务。
- 任务反映的是职位描述中具体的工作内容，而非广义的角色描述。
- 每个任务有且仅有一个 skill_group_id。

A.2 第二阶段提示：暴露分类
你是生成式AI领域的专家。你的任务是根据工作任务受生成式AI/大语言模型工具影响的程度对其进行分类。
假设：
- 该角色中具有平均专业水平的工人。
- 可以使用强大LLM和现成的生成式AI工具。
- 可以使用标准笔记本电脑工具（例如麦克风、扬声器）。
- 除笔记本电脑外，无物理工具或物理在场要求。

【本段术语】
- Generative AI: 生成式AI
- LLM: 大语言模型
- JSON: JSON（保留英文）
- task: 任务
- posting: 职位公告/招聘信息
- skill group: 技能组
- skill_group_id: skill_group_id（保留英文）
- posting_id: posting_id（保留英文）
- posting_title: posting_title（保留英文）
- group_id: group_id（保留英文）
- task_id: task_id（保留英文）
- NS0: NS0（保留英文）
- S1, C1: S1, C1（保留英文）

【本段要点】
- 给出了任务提取、技能组匹配和JSON输出格式的严格规则。
- 强调任务必须基于正文，避免无关信息；匹配时优先选择专业组。
- 第二阶段提示要求基于生成式AI/LLM能力对工作任务进行暴露分类，并设定了工人能力和工具的假设条件。

【可能需人工复核】
- “posting”一词在中文语境中可能有“招聘信息”“职位描述”“岗位公告”等译法，此处统一采用“职位描述”或“招聘信息”均合理，但需确保全篇一致。
- “exposure”在AI暴露语境下常译为“暴露度”或“受影响程度”，此处译为“暴露”可能需根据后续上下文确认是否调整。
- “skill_group_id”“posting_id”等JSON键名保留英文，但读者是否理解需评估。
- 原文中“A.2 Stage 2 Prompt”在附录中，标题格式需与整体附录结构一致。

## English

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

Task extraction rules: - Tasks must be grounded in the BODY text and reflect real actions, tools, systems, materials, interactions, or work settings mentioned. - Preserve specificity whenever possible (software names, equipment, documents, samples, customers, patients, systems, environments). - Focus on observable actions (clear verbs + objects). - Only include tasks explicitly stated or clearly implied by the BODY text. STRICTLY AVOID: - Company information, compensation, benefits, qualifications, or hiring instructions. -------------------------------------------------STEP 3. Match Tasks to Skill Groups -------------------------------------------------- Assign EACH task exactly ONE skill_group_id. - Compare the task against all skill groups (specialized + common). - Choose the closest semantic match. - In case of ties, prefer specialized groups (S*) over common groups (C*). - If no skills exist, assign all tasks to NS0. -------------------------------------------------OUTPUT FORMAT (STRICT — JSON ONLY) -------------------------------------------------Return EXACTLY one JSON object with this schema: { "posting_id": "<ID>", "posting_title": "<TITLE_NAME>", "skills_groups": [ {"group_id": "S1", "group_skills": ["..."]}, {"group_id": "C1", "group_skills": ["..."]}, {"group_id": "NS0", "group_skills": []} ], "tasks": [ { "task_id": "t1", "task": "<8–50-word posting-specific task>", "skill_group_id": "S1 | C1 | NS0" } ] } FINAL CHECKS: - Valid JSON only. - 3–10 tasks. - Tasks reflect concrete work described in the posting, not generalized role descriptions. - Every task has exactly one skill_group_id. A. 2 Stage 2 Prompt: Exposure Classification You are an expert on Generative AI. Your task is to classify work tasks by their exposure to GenAI/LLM tools. Assume: - A worker with average expertise in this role. - Access to powerful LLMs and readily available GenAI tools. - Access to standard laptop tools (e. g., microphone, speakers). - NO physical tools or physical presence beyond a laptop.

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

## 中文

【中文译文】

# 附录A 完整注释提示

你将收到一个JSON对象，包含：
- posting_id: 字符串。职位发布ID。
- posting_title: 字符串。职位名称。
- tasks: 任务对象列表，每个任务包含：
  - task_id: 字符串（例如"t1"）
  - task: 描述工作者任务活动的字符串。

请为每个任务分配一个且仅一个暴露标签，标签取自 {"E0", "E1", "E2"}：

E0（无暴露）：
- 如果现有的GenAI/LLM工具（ChatGPT、辅助编程工具、ASR/TTS、多模态工具）无法以同等质量将任务时间减少50%，则标记为E0。
- 需要大量面对面互动、物理操作、检查、维修、现场护理或受资格认证约束决策的任务必须为E0。

E1（直接暴露）：
- 如果单个现成的GenAI/LLM工具（无需特殊集成或微调）能够以同等质量将任务工作量减少50%，则标记为E1。
- 典型的E1模式（非详尽）：
  * 编写或转换文本或代码
  * 翻译、语气/风格编辑
  * 对中等长度文档进行摘要；提取结构化信息
  * 根据提供的内容起草电子邮件、简报、幻灯片、问答
  * ASR转录；TTS草稿旁白；简单的音频清理
  * 简单的图像生成/编辑（缩略图、字幕、营销图片）
- 不适用E1的情况：需要内部数据访问、企业系统、自定义工作流或超出复制粘贴范围的自动化任务。

E2（LLM+暴露）：
- 如果单个现成的GenAI/LLM工具本身无法实现50%的时间减少，但一个浅层的AI驱动软件层有可能实现这一目标，则标记为E2。
- 浅层软件层的示例：
  * 对私有/内部文档的检索引擎或搜索
  * 多步骤工作流（草稿→审查→格式化→上传）
  * 产品内助手（CRM、IDE、帮助台）读取上下文并建议操作/回复
  * 客服系统中的自动建议回复
  * 评分标准/政策/品牌执行；轻量级微调
  * 集成到资产库或翻译流程的多模态工具
- 不适用E2的情况：
  * 如果已适用E1 → 选择E1
  * 即使通过集成，AI也无法合理地将时间减半 → 选择E0
  * 需要大量定制机器学习、机器人或新模型训练 → 选择E0

输出格式（严格）：
返回一个JSON对象：
{
  "posting_id": "<与输入相同>",
  "task_exposures": [
    {"task_id": "t1", "exposure_label": "E1"},
    {"task_id": "t2", "exposure_label": "E0"}
  ]
}

规则：
- 仅返回有效JSON。不包含解释或额外文本。
- 每个输入task_id必须恰好出现一次。
- exposure_label必须是"E0"、"E1"或"E2"中的一个。

【本段术语】
- GPT: [待定]
- GenAI: [待定]
- LLM: [待定]
- ChatGPT: [待定]
- ASR: [待定]（自动语音识别）
- TTS: [待定]（文本转语音）
- CRM: [待定]（客户关系管理）
- IDE: [待定]（集成开发环境）
- tagging: [待定]

【本段要点】
- 本附录描述了为任务分配生成式AI暴露等级（E0、E1、E2）的注释提示。
- E0表示现有GenAI/LLM工具无法将任务时间减少50%且无需实质性物理交互。
- E1表示单个现成工具可直接减少50%工作量，典型场景包括文本/代码处理、翻译、摘要等。
- E2表示需通过浅层AI软件集成（如检索、多步骤工作流、产品内助手）才能实现50%时间缩减。
- 输出必须为严格格式的JSON，每个任务ID出现一次，标签仅限E0/E1/E2。

【可能需人工复核】
- 术语表中大量术语为[待定]，需根据上下文决定中文译名，例如"GenAI"译为"生成式AI"或保留英文，"ASR/TTS"需确定标准译名。
- "thin AI-powered software layer"译为"浅层的AI驱动软件层"是否准确，或"轻量AI软件层"更优？
- "copy-paste"是否应保留为"复制粘贴"或更专业的"剪贴板操作"？
- 规则中"Return ONLY valid JSON"强调整体输出格式，但中文翻译中需确保JSON结构不被破坏。

## English

# Appendix A Full Annotation Prompts

You will receive ONE JSON object containing: - posting_id: string. Job posting ID. - posting_title: string. Job title. - tasks: list of task objects, each with: - task_id: string (e. g., "t1") - task: string describing the worker task activity. Assign exactly ONE exposure_label to each task in { "E0", "E1", "E2" }: E0 (No exposure): - Label E0 if readily available GenAI/LLM tools (ChatGPT, copilots, ASR/TTS, multimodal tools) cannot reduce task time by ￿50% at equivalent quality. - Tasks requiring substantial in-person interaction, physical manipulation, inspections, repairs, hands-on care, or credential-bound decisions must be E0. E1 (Direct exposure): - Label E1 if a single off-the-shelf GenAI/LLM tool, with no special integrations or fine-tuning, can reduce effort by ￿50% at equivalent quality. - Typical E1 patterns (not exhaustive): * Writing or transforming text or code * Translation, tone/style edits * Summarizing medium-length documents; extracting structured info * Drafting emails, briefs, slides, Q&A based on provided content * ASR transcription; TTS draft narration; simple audio clean-up * Simple image generation/editing (thumbnails, captions, marketing images) - Not E1: tasks needing internal data access, enterprise systems, custom workflows, or automation beyond copy-paste. E2 (LLM+ exposure): - Label E2 if a single off-the-shelf GenAI/LLM tool alone cannot achieve ￿50% time reduction, but a thin AI-powered software layer could plausibly do so. - Examples of thin layers: * Retrieval or search over private/internal documents * Multi-step workflows (draft → review → format → upload) * In-product assist (CRM, IDE, helpdesk) that reads context and suggests actions/replies. * Auto-suggest replies in customer service systems * Rubric/policy/brand enforcement; light fine-tuning * Integrated multimodal tools tied to asset libraries or translation pipelines - Not E2: * If E1 already applies → choose E1 * If even with integration AI cannot plausibly halve time → choose E0 * If heavy bespoke ML, robotics, or new model training is required → choose E0 OUTPUT FORMAT (STRICT): Return ONE JSON object: { "posting_id": "<same as input>", "task_exposures": [ {"task_id": "t1", "exposure_label": "E1"}, {"task_id": "t2", "exposure_label": "E0"} ] } Rules: - Return ONLY valid JSON. No explanation or extra text. - Every input task_id must appear exactly once. - exposure_label must be exactly one of "E0", "E1", or "E2".

# Appendix B Comparison with Eloundou et al. (2024)

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 附录B 与Eloundou等人(2024)的比较

为将我们的测量方法与现有文献进行对标，我们将基于岗位的暴露度测量与Eloundou等人(2024)基于职业层面的暴露度测量进行比较。后者的测量源自O*NET任务数据，为每个职业分配一个固定不变的暴露得分；而我们的测量则基于岗位招聘数据，能够反映同一职业内不同岗位之间以及随时间变化的异质性。为使两种方法具有可比性，我们将岗位层面的暴露度测量β_p聚合至职业层面，并与Eloundou等人(2024)的基准进行比较。图B1显示，全样本职业层面平均后的我们的测量值与Eloundou等人(2024)的基准高度相关。因此，在职业层面的聚合程度上，我们的测量与Eloundou等人(2024)的基准大致一致。然而，这种聚合比较掩盖了单一职业层面得分无法捕捉的两个异质性维度。第一，在同一职业内，不同资历水平的暴露度存在差异。第二，职业层面的暴露度本身随时间演变。这些额外维度与附录图D3–D6中更广泛的描述性证据一致，该证据显示暴露度因职业组、资历水平和时间而异。

【本段术语】
- posting-based exposure measure: 基于岗位的暴露度测量
- occupation-level exposure measure: 职业层面的暴露度测量
- O*NET: O*NET（职业信息网络）
- posting-level exposure measure: 岗位层面的暴露度测量
- β_p: β_p（岗位层面暴露度系数）
- full-sample occupation-level average: 全样本职业层面平均值
- benchmark: 基准
- heterogeneity: 异质性
- seniority levels: 资历水平
- within the same occupation: 同一职业内
- occupation-level exposure: 职业层面暴露度
- time-invariant exposure score: 固定不变的暴露得分
- job postings: 岗位招聘数据

【本段要点】
- 与Eloundou等人(2024)的职业层面暴露度测量进行比较。
- 聚合至职业层面后，本测量与基准高度相关，表明总体一致性。
- 但聚合比较掩盖了两个异质性维度：同一职业内不同资历水平的差异以及职业层面暴露度随时间的演变。
- 这些异质性在附录图D3–D6中有进一步描述性证据支持。

【可能需人工复核】
- 术语"暴露度"是否准确传达"exposure"含义，需结合领域惯例确认。
- 原文中"posting-level"和"occupation-level"的翻译选择是否一致。

## English

# Appendix B Comparison with Eloundou et al. (2024)

To benchmark our measure against the existing literature, we compare our posting-based exposure measure with the occupation-level exposure measure in Eloundou et al. (2024). Their measure is constructed from O*NET task data and assigns each occupation a single, time-invariant exposure score, whereas our measure is constructed from job postings and can vary across postings within the same occupation and over time. To make the two approaches comparable, we aggregate our posting-level exposure measure β p to the occupation level and compare it with the benchmark in Eloundou et al. (2024). Figure B1 shows that the full-sample occupation-level average of our measure is highly correlated with the benchmark in Eloundou et al. (2024). Thus, at the aggregate occupation level, our measure is broadly aligned with the benchmark in Eloundou et al. (2024). However, thisaggregatecomparisonmaskstwodimensionsofheterogeneitythatasingleoccupationlevelscorecannotcapture. First, exposurediffersacrosssenioritylevelswithinthesameoccupation. Second, occupation-level exposure itself evolves over time. These additional margins are consistent withthebroaderdescriptiveevidenceinAppendixFiguresD3–D6, whichshowthatexposurevaries across occupation groups, seniority levels, and time.

# Figure B2 summarizes these two additional dimensions directly. Panel (a) plots, for each occu-

## 中文

【中文译文】
图B2直接总结了这两个额外维度。图(a)展示了每个职业中，高级岗位发布与初级岗位发布的平均暴露度之差。该分布的中心位于零值以上，表明即使在同一职业内部，高级岗位发布的暴露度也往往高于初级岗位。图(b)展示了职业层面暴露度随时间的变化：首先将暴露度汇总至职业-季度层面，然后对每个季度内的所有职业取平均值。该时间序列表明，职业层面暴露度并非固定不变，而是随时间逐渐变化。综合来看，这些结果证明，我们的度量在总体职业层面与Eloundou et al. (2024)的基准保持一致，同时额外捕捉了职业内部因资历导致的异质性以及职业内部随时间的变化。

【本段术语】
- Figure B2: 图B2
- occupation: 职业
- exposure: 暴露度
- senior postings: 高级岗位发布
- junior postings: 初级岗位发布
- occupation-level exposure: 职业层面暴露度
- occupation-by-quarter: 职业-季度
- within-occupation: 职业内部
- seniority: 资历
- Eloundou et al. (2024): Eloundou等人（2024）

【本段要点】
- 图B2(a)显示高级岗位比初级岗位暴露度更高，即便在同一职业内部。
- 图B2(b)显示职业层面暴露度随时间逐渐变化，并非固定。
- 作者的度量在总体层面与既有基准一致，并额外捕捉到职业内部的资历异质性和时间变化。

【可能需人工复核】
- "posting" 在此上下文中译为“岗位发布”是否准确？亦可考虑“招聘广告”或“职位发布”，需根据全文语境统一。
- “exposure” 译为“暴露度”是否符合该领域惯例？文中reference为 Eloundou et al. (2024)，若其使用“exposure”特指AI暴露程度，则此译法可接受。
- 图B2(b)中“first aggregated to the occupation-by-quarter level”的“aggregated”译为“汇总”准确，但需注意“occupation-by-quarter level”是否应译为“职业-季度层面”或“按职业与季度汇总的层面”。此处保留连字符以强调数据类型。

## English

# Figure B2 summarizes these two additional dimensions directly. Panel (a) plots, for each occu-

pation, the difference between the average exposure of senior postings and that of junior postings. The distribution is centered above zero, indicating that senior postings tend to be more exposed than junior postings even within the same occupation. Panel (b) plots the evolution of occupationlevel exposure over time, where exposure is first aggregated to the occupation-by-quarter level and then averaged across occupations within each quarter. This time series shows that occupation-level exposure is not fixed, but instead changes gradually over time. Taken together, these results show that our measure is consistent with the benchmark in Eloundou et al. (2024) at the aggregate occupation level, while additionally capturing within-occupation heterogeneity by seniority and within-occupation changes over time.

# Figure B2: Additional Heterogeneity Captured by the Posting-Based Measure

## 中文

【中文译文】
# 图B2：基于岗位发布测量所捕捉的额外异质性

注释：图(a)展示了 \(\bar{\beta}_{o, \text{senior}} - \bar{\beta}_{o, \text{junior}}\) 的分布，其中 \(\bar{\beta}_{o, \text{senior}}\) 和 \(\bar{\beta}_{o, \text{junior}}\) 分别表示职业 \(o\) 内高级岗位发布与初级岗位发布的平均暴露度。正值表明同一职业内高级岗位的暴露度高于初级岗位。图(b)展示了职业层面暴露度随时间的变化。对于每个季度 \(t\)，我们首先计算每个职业 \(o\) 内的平均暴露度，然后对这些职业层面的均值按职业取平均：\(\bar{\beta}_t = \frac{1}{|O_t|} \sum_{o \in O_t} \bar{\beta}_{o,t}\)。该图表明，职业层面暴露度随时间 \(t\) 演变，而非固定为某个单一的职业特定值。

【本段术语】
- posting-based measure: [待定]
- occupation-level exposure: [待定]
- senior postings: [待定]
- junior postings: [待定]
- within the same occupation: [待定]

【本段要点】
- 图(a)通过比较同一职业内高级与初级岗位的平均暴露度差异，揭示了基于岗位发布测量所捕获的职业内部异质性。
- 图(b)展示了职业层面平均暴露度随时间（按季度）的变化趋势，说明暴露度并非静态的职业固定值，而是动态演变的。

【可能需人工复核】
- 术语表中“posting-based measure”“occupation-level exposure”等中文翻译需最终确认。
- 公式 \(\bar{\beta}_t\) 的表达在原文中有笔误（如“t∑mean”），译文已按语义修正，建议核对原始数据图注。
